## Historical information

### Date founded

c. [5000 BBY](/wiki/5000_BBY "5000 BBY"),[[39]](#cite_note-Timelines-39) from a [Jedi splinter group](/wiki/Jedi_splinter_group "Jedi splinter group")[[40]](#cite_note-Sith-40)

### Location of origin

Moraband[[17]](#cite_note-Sacrifice-17)

* After 4 [ABY](/wiki/Galactic_standard_calendar "Galactic standard calendar")[[42]](#cite_note-GA-42)

[[Source]](https://starwars.fandom.com/wiki/Template:Religion)

:   "*They hoped to fill me with fear. But fear leads to anger. Anger leads to hate. And hate…leads to power.*"
:   ―Darth Vader[[45]](#cite_note-Darth_Vader_(2020)_10-45)

The **Sith**, also referred to as the **Sith Order**, was an ancient [religious](/wiki/Religion "Religion") order of [Force-wielders](/wiki/Force-sensitive "Force-sensitive") devoted to the [dark side of the Force](/wiki/Dark_side_of_the_Force "Dark side of the Force"). Driven by their emotions, including hate, anger, and greed, the Sith were deceptive and obsessed with gaining power no matter the cost. The order had many forms until it reached the apex of its power under [Darth Sidious](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious"), the [Dark Lord of the Sith](/wiki/Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith "Dark Lord of the Sith") who achieved his order's goal of [galactic](/wiki/Galaxy "Galaxy") conquest after a [millennium](/wiki/Millennium "Millennium") of [plotting](/wiki/Grand_Plan "Grand Plan"). Within a generation, however, the [deaths](/wiki/Death "Death") of Darth Sidious and [Darth Vader](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker") marked the end of the [Sith Lords](/wiki/Sith_Lord "Sith Lord"). Though the Sith went extinct, they still had a powerful legacy, and many continued to follow their teachings. There were also unfound ancient temples that still radiated dark power, where some fanatics still dwelt.

Thousands of [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") before the [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars"), the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order") was fractured by a [schism](/wiki/Hundred-Year_Darkness "Hundred-Year Darkness") that began when a [rogue Jedi](/wiki/Unidentified_rogue_Jedi "Unidentified rogue Jedi") and his [followers](/wiki/Jedi_splinter_group "Jedi splinter group") turned away from the [light side of the Force](/wiki/Light_side_of_the_Force "Light side of the Force"), believing the dark side was the path to true power. Having relocated to the [planet](/wiki/Planet "Planet") [Korriban](/wiki/Moraband "Moraband") in the [Outer Rim Territories](/wiki/Outer_Rim_Territories "Outer Rim Territories"), their movement ultimately evolved into the Sith Order, resulting in a [war](/wiki/Sith_war_(Old_Republic) "Sith war (Old Republic)") between the former brothers and sisters in [the Force](/wiki/The_Force "The Force") as the [Jedi Knights](/wiki/Jedi_Knight "Jedi Knight") rallied to the defense of the [Old Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic"). Although the Sith were driven off of the [Core World](/wiki/Core_Worlds "Core Worlds") [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant "Coruscant") by [5000 BBY](/wiki/5000_BBY "5000 BBY"), [centuries](/wiki/Standard_century "Standard century") of conflict ensued between the two orders, culminating in the Old Republic's [collapse](/wiki/Fall_of_the_Old_Republic "Fall of the Old Republic"). Undermined by constant infighting and ruined by the [last war](/wiki/Jedi-Sith_War "Jedi-Sith War") against the [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi"), the Sith were rendered all but extinct with the exception of one; [Darth Bane](/wiki/Darth_Bane "Darth Bane") survived the ancient order's destruction and passed his knowledge to a single apprentice, [Darth Zannah](/wiki/Darth_Zannah "Darth Zannah"), before being entombed on Korriban, which became known as Moraband. Henceforth, the Sith was governed by the [Rule of Two](/wiki/Rule_of_Two "Rule of Two"), a new philosophy dictating that only two Sith [Lords](/wiki/Lord "Lord")—a [Sith Master](/wiki/Sith_Master "Sith Master") and a [Sith apprentice](/wiki/Sith_apprentice "Sith apprentice")—could exist at any given [time](/wiki/Time "Time"). As a result, the Sith were all but forgotten while the Jedi focused their efforts on [preserving](/wiki/Law_enforcement_agency "Law enforcement agency") the [new age of peace](/wiki/Republic_Era "Republic Era") under the modern Galactic Republic.

The Sith remained in hiding for a millennium until the rise of [Darth](/wiki/Darth "Darth") Sidious and [Darth Maul](/wiki/Maul "Maul") in [32 BBY](/wiki/32_BBY "32 BBY"). Sidious, trained by [Darth Plagueis](/wiki/Darth_Plagueis "Darth Plagueis"), hid in plain sight as [Senator](/wiki/Senator "Senator") Sheev Palpatine of [Naboo](/wiki/Naboo "Naboo"). Orchestrating the [blockade](/wiki/Blockade "Blockade") and [invasion](/wiki/Invasion_of_Naboo "Invasion of Naboo") of his [homeworld](/wiki/Homeworld "Homeworld") by the [Trade Federation](/wiki/Trade_Federation "Trade Federation"), Sidious maneuvered the [Galactic Senate](/wiki/Galactic_Senate "Galactic Senate") into electing him to the [office](/wiki/Office_of_the_Chancellor "Office of the Chancellor") of [Supreme Chancellor](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor "Supreme Chancellor"). His entire chancellery would encompass the [final years](/wiki/Republic_Era "Republic Era") of the Republic. Over the next [decade](/wiki/Standard_decade "Standard decade") Sidious sowed the seeds of discontent within the galactic populace with the help of his new apprentice, the former [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") [Count](/wiki/Count "Count") [Dooku](/wiki/Dooku "Dooku"), who adopted the name of Darth Tyranus and became the public face of the [Independent Movement for Self-Determination](/wiki/Independent_Movement_for_Self-Determination "Independent Movement for Self-Determination"). The [Separatist Crisis](/wiki/Separatist_Crisis "Separatist Crisis") culminated in the formation of the [Confederacy of Independent Systems](/wiki/Confederacy_of_Independent_Systems "Confederacy of Independent Systems") and the creation of the [Separatist Droid Army](/wiki/Separatist_Droid_Army "Separatist Droid Army") which, in turn, compelled the Senate to support the establishment of the [Grand Army of the Republic](/wiki/Grand_Army_of_the_Republic "Grand Army of the Republic"). [Jar Jar Binks](/wiki/Jar_Jar_Binks "Jar Jar Binks"), acting in place of Senator [Amidala](/wiki/Padm%C3%A9_Amidala "Padmé Amidala"), started a motion to grant the [Supreme Chancellor](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor "Supreme Chancellor") emergency powers.

The [Clone](/wiki/Cloning "Cloning") Wars began with the [First Battle of Geonosis](/wiki/First_Battle_of_Geonosis "First Battle of Geonosis") in [22 BBY](/wiki/22_BBY "22 BBY"), after which entire [armies](/wiki/Army "Army") of [battle droids](/wiki/Battle_droid "Battle droid") and [clone troopers](/wiki/Clone_trooper "Clone trooper") deployed across [the galaxy](/wiki/The_galaxy "The galaxy"), making war and devastation commonplace for the first time since the [formation of the Republic](/wiki/1032_BBY "1032 BBY"). In the final [months](/wiki/Standard_month "Standard month") of the Clone Wars, Sidious [sacrificed](/wiki/Battle_of_Coruscant "Battle of Coruscant") and betrayed Tyranus as part of his plot to turn Anakin Skywalker, the Jedi Order's prophesied [Chosen One](/wiki/Chosen_One "Chosen One"), to the dark side. Playing on Skywalker's fear of losing his secret [wife](/wiki/Marriage "Marriage"), Senator [Padmé Amidala](/wiki/Padm%C3%A9_Amidala "Padmé Amidala"), Palpatine revealed his deception and true identity, while claiming that the dark side was the path to [immortality](/wiki/Immortality "Immortality"). Members of the [Jedi High Council](/wiki/Jedi_High_Council "Jedi High Council"), having learned from Skywalker's report that the chancellor was, in fact, a Sith Lord, attempted to [arrest](/wiki/Prison "Prison") Palpatine, but the chancellor resisted. Torn between his faith in the Jedi and the fate he foresaw for his wife, Skywalker ultimately chose the Sith by betraying [Mace Windu](/wiki/Mace_Windu "Mace Windu"), allowing Sidious to kill the Jedi Order's great champion.

Using the [incident](/wiki/Duel_in_Palpatine%27s_office "Duel in Palpatine's office") in the [chancellor's office](/wiki/Emperor%27s_office "Emperor's office") to frame the Jedi Order for [treason](/wiki/Treason "Treason"), Sidious declared [Order 66](/wiki/Order_66 "Order 66") was in effect, marking all Jedi as enemies of the state. The clone [troopers](/wiki/Trooper "Trooper")' [programming](/wiki/Behavioral_modification_biochip "Behavioral modification biochip") turned them against their [Jedi Generals](/wiki/Jedi_General "Jedi General"), who were betrayed and [executed](/wiki/Death_penalty "Death penalty") across the galaxy. With the majority of the order falling victim to the [Great Jedi Purge](/wiki/Great_Jedi_Purge "Great Jedi Purge"), Sidious [announced](/wiki/Proclamation_of_the_New_Order "Proclamation of the New Order") the creation of a [new regime](/wiki/New_Order "New Order"), transforming the Republic into the [First Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire") in [19 BBY](/wiki/19_BBY "19 BBY"). With the former Anakin Skywalker, renamed Darth Vader, at his side, the self-proclaimed [Galactic Emperor](/wiki/Galactic_Emperor "Galactic Emperor")'s rise to power was complete, and the Sith were restored to dominance after centuries of plotting.

The Sith's control of the galaxy remained relatively unchallenged for a [generation](/wiki/Imperial_Era "Imperial Era") until the [birth](/wiki/Declaration_of_Rebellion "Declaration of Rebellion") of the [Alliance to Restore the Republic](/wiki/Alliance_to_Restore_the_Republic "Alliance to Restore the Republic") which, in turn, led to the [Galactic Civil War](/wiki/Galactic_Civil_War "Galactic Civil War") in [1 BBY](/wiki/1_BBY "1 BBY"). The Emperor, having felt a [disturbance in the Force](/wiki/Disturbance_in_the_Force "Disturbance in the Force"), discovered that his apprentice's long lost [son](/wiki/Skywalker_family "Skywalker family"), [Luke Skywalker](/wiki/Luke_Skywalker "Luke Skywalker"), was [training](/wiki/Jedi_training "Jedi training") to become a Jedi. Aware of the potential Luke inherited from his [father](/wiki/Parent "Parent"), the Emperor foresaw the possibility of his own destruction but resolved to turn the young man to the dark side as he did with Vader. During the [Battle of Endor](/wiki/Battle_of_Endor "Battle of Endor") in [4 ABY](/wiki/4_ABY "4 ABY"), the Emperor forced father and son into a [duel](/wiki/Lightsaber_duel "Lightsaber duel"), which ended with Luke disarming Vader. The Emperor subsequently betrayed Vader by ordering Luke to finish him off and be Sidious's apprentice, but the young Jedi Knight refused. Knowing he had lost Luke to the Jedi, the Emperor proceeded to [torture](/wiki/Torture "Torture") Luke with torrents of [Force lightning](/wiki/Force_lightning "Force lightning"). At that moment, Vader, overwhelmed by his son's compassion for him, chose to save Luke by killing his master.

The death of the now redeemed Anakin Skywalker, marked the extinction of the Sith, who then succumbed to his injuries—bringing balance to the Force. Yet while the ancient [Chosen One](/wiki/Chosen_One "Chosen One") prophecy foretold the Sith's demise, it never predicted the end of the dark side. With wielders continuing to endure, such as the [Nightsisters](/wiki/Nightsisters "Nightsisters") or [Knights of Ren](/wiki/Knights_of_Ren "Knights of Ren"). After the [First Order](/wiki/First_Order "First Order") [rise](/wiki/Cold_War "Cold War") from the [Unknown Regions](/wiki/Unknown_Regions "Unknown Regions"), the enigmatic darksider [Supreme Leader](/wiki/Supreme_Leader "Supreme Leader") [Snoke](/wiki/Snoke "Snoke") [throne](/wiki/Throne "Throne") was [succeeded](/wiki/Battle_of_Oetchi "Battle of Oetchi") by [Kylo Ren](/wiki/Ben_Solo "Ben Solo")—nephew of [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") Skywalker during the [war](/wiki/First_Order-Resistance_War "First Order-Resistance War") against the [Resistance](/wiki/Resistance "Resistance"). Snoke was in fact only a [creation and tool](/wiki/Strand-Cast "Strand-Cast") of a reborn Darth Sidious after he [announced](/wiki/Palpatine%27s_broadcast "Palpatine's broadcast") his return to the galaxy and revealed the [Final Order](/wiki/Final_Order "Final Order"). The clone emperor and his cults—the [Sith Eternal](/wiki/Sith_Eternal "Sith Eternal") emergence from hiding resulted in a desperate final [battle](/wiki/Battle_of_Exegol "Battle of Exegol") against the him which saw the Jedi [Rey](/wiki/Rey_Skywalker "Rey Skywalker") and a redeemed Ben Solo to destroy Sidious, permanently preventing the rebirth of the Sith.

## Philosophy[]

### The Code of the Sith[]

:   "*Anger and pain are natural and part of growth. They give you focus. They make you strong.*"
:   ―Darth Vader[[27]](#cite_note-Backstories_Vader-27)

 [![Generations of Sith adhered to a philosophy of power through the dark side of the Force.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e2/DarthVader22.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180724184711) [![Generations of Sith adhered to a philosophy of power through the dark side of the Force.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e2/DarthVader22.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180724184711)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e2/DarthVader22.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20180724184711) 

Generations of Sith adhered to a philosophy of power through the dark side of the Force.

 

The Sith focused on primal emotions like anger and pain in order to gain power from the [dark side of the Force](/wiki/Dark_side_of_the_Force "Dark side of the Force"). The [Code of the Sith](/wiki/Code_of_the_Sith "Code of the Sith") was the antithesis of the [Jedi Code](/wiki/Jedi_Code "Jedi Code"), although like its counterpart, it governed the actions and beliefs of the Sith. The Sith code insisted on the importance of passion and the rejection of peace.[[27]](#cite_note-Backstories_Vader-27)

:   *Peace is a lie. There is only passion.*
:   *Through passion I gain strength.*
:   *Through strength I gain power.*
:   *Through power I gain victory.*
:   *Through victory my chains are broken.*
:   *The Force shall free me.*[[28]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Sith-28)

The Sith wore [clothing](/wiki/Clothing "Clothing") that obscured their identity while in hiding.[[38]](#cite_note-VE-38) They used the term "dark side" because they were secretive. The Sith felt it was easier to impose order if they kept their identities and knowledge a secret or, as [Lona Aphra](/wiki/Lona_Aphra "Lona Aphra") put it, "hidden—in the dark."[[46]](#cite_note-Aphra_32-46) The [hex charm](/wiki/Sith_Eternal_crest "Sith Eternal crest") was a traditional symbol of the Sith.[[26]](#cite_note-Shadow_of_the_Sith-26) [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") [Zallah Macri](/wiki/Zallah_Macri "Zallah Macri") maintained that, in the abstract, the Sith Order's ideals may have seemed "good" to a Jedi, but the finer details and their actions painted a clearer picture for what they truly stood for.[[47]](#cite_note-POD-47) Indeed, many who joined the Sith[[24]](#cite_note-Episode_III-24) or related dark side groups tried to rationalize their actions at first[[48]](#cite_note-The_Fallen_Star-48) before being fully consumed by the dark side.[[24]](#cite_note-Episode_III-24)

### The Doctrine of the Dyad[]

:   "*The Doctrine of the Dyad was etched into the walls of my citadel on Exegol eons ago, a constant reminder of its significance to our Order. To my Sith Eternal, the dyad is not merely the stuff of ancient legend; it is the future of the Sith—the key to unlocking the full potential of the dark side.*"
:   ―Darth Sidious[[28]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Sith-28)

 [![The Doctrine of the Dyad preceded the Sith Order's Rule of Two.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6d/Dyad.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20211012225649) [![The Doctrine of the Dyad preceded the Sith Order's Rule of Two.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6d/Dyad.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20211012225649)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6d/Dyad.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20211012225649) 

The Doctrine of the Dyad preceded the Sith Order's Rule of Two.

 

The [Doctrine of the Dyad](/wiki/Doctrine_of_the_Dyad "Doctrine of the Dyad") arose from the concept of a [Force dyad](/wiki/Force_dyad "Force dyad"). A dyad was a powerful [Force-bond](/wiki/Force-bond "Force-bond") connecting two [Force-sensitives](/wiki/Force-sensitive "Force-sensitive"); the bond transcended their physical beings and combined them into one presence in [the Force](/wiki/The_Force "The Force"). The beings in a dyad possessed rare abilities that were unique to their bond, and therefore unattainable to those who lacked a dyadic connection, regardless of their own strength or experience with the Force. Over the generations, the Sith sought in vain to create a dyad through sheer willpower, believing it was the key to achieving the ultimate power of the dark side. The [Sith Lord](/wiki/Sith_Lord "Sith Lord") [Darth Sidious](/wiki/Darth_Sidious "Darth Sidious") viewed the dyad as a source of limitless power.[[28]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Sith-28)

The Doctrine of the Dyad was etched into the walls of the [Sith Citadel](/wiki/Sith_Citadel "Sith Citadel") on [Exegol](/wiki/Exegol "Exegol"), eons before Sidious' time, to remind the Sith of the dyad's significance to their Order.[[28]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Sith-28) The Doctrine of the Dyad also influenced the [Sith Eternal](/wiki/Sith_Eternal "Sith Eternal"), a [cult](/wiki/Sith_cult "Sith cult") of [Sith devotees](/wiki/Sith_cultist "Sith cultist") who [predicted](/wiki/Doctrine_of_the_Dyad "Doctrine of the Dyad") the return of the dyad.[[4]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-4) Like the Sith Order, the Sith Eternal believed that the dyad was essential to realizing the dark side's full potential.[[28]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Sith-28)

### The Rule of Two[]

:   "*But there was a Sith Lord who survived the culling—the great Darth Bane. It was he who reshaped the Sith, creating a new hierarchy to ensure the survival of our Order. His Rule of Two dictated that only two Sith Lords could exist at any one time—a master to possess the unlimited power of the dark side and an apprentice to covet it.*"
:   ―Darth Sidious[[28]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Sith-28)

 [![The Rule of Two governed the Sith Order for a millennium, from its ancient founder to the last Dark Lord of the Sith.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a3/SithOrder-SOTJ.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200113231523) [![The Rule of Two governed the Sith Order for a millennium, from its ancient founder to the last Dark Lord of the Sith.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a3/SithOrder-SOTJ.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200113231523)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a3/SithOrder-SOTJ.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200113231523) 

The Rule of Two governed the Sith Order for a millennium, from its ancient founder to the last Dark Lord of the Sith.

 

Even before the formation of the [Rule of Two](/wiki/Rule_of_Two "Rule of Two") that decreed only two Sith—a [Sith Master](/wiki/Sith_Master "Sith Master") and a [Sith apprentice](/wiki/Sith_apprentice "Sith apprentice")—could exist at one time,[[28]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Sith-28) the Sith of old often found themselves ruled by two Sith in specific, who would reign over their many fellow Sith.[[49]](#cite_note-TROS_JN-49) The Rule of Two, however, would officially limit the Sith Order's numbers due to the infighting that had ruined it. The rule nonetheless ensured the relationship between a Sith Master and their apprentice was not one of trust; indeed, both the master and the apprentice constantly searched for any sign of weakness in the other, for a weak master deserved to be overthrown by their pupil, just as a weak pupil deserved to be replaced by a worthier, more powerful recruit. This philosophy was embraced by the Sith, who adopted it as a way to purify the weak and become stronger over time, since only an apprentice who had surpassed all previous Sith could take their master's place through honorable combat.[[27]](#cite_note-Backstories_Vader-27)

The Sith were free to train dark side agents identified as [Sith acolytes](/wiki/Sith_acolyte "Sith acolyte")[[50]](#cite_note-Dark_Disciple-50) so long as those acolytes were not trained as true Sith Lords. However, it was more than possible the Sith apprentice would violate the Rule of Two by training an acolyte as a real apprentice, intending to have their aid in overthrowing the Sith Master.[[51]](#cite_note-Nightsisters-51) The concept of the dyad influenced the philosophy of the Rule of Two, emphasized the power of two Force-sensitives working in tandem to grow even more powerful as an Order. As the successor of the Doctrine of the Dyad, the Rule of Two was seen as a "pale imitation" of its predecessor by Darth Sidious.[[28]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Sith-28)

## History[]

### Ancient times[]

#### The Hundred-Year Darkness[]

:   "*Once we were brothers in the Force. But from the Hundred-Year Darkness were born the Sith.*"
:   ―Unidentified Jedi[[52]](#cite_note-SW9-52)

 [![Korriban, later known as Moraband, was settled by the Sith following their schism with the Jedi Order.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9e/Moraband_Planet.png/revision/latest?cb=20200224011130) [![Korriban, later known as Moraband, was settled by the Sith following their schism with the Jedi Order.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9e/Moraband_Planet.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/180?cb=20200224011130)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/9e/Moraband_Planet.png/revision/latest?cb=20200224011130) 

Korriban, later known as Moraband, was settled by the Sith following their schism with the Jedi Order.

 

Formed around [5000 BBY](/wiki/5000_BBY "5000 BBY")[[39]](#cite_note-Timelines-39), the Sith were the ancient enemies of the [Jedi Order](/wiki/Jedi_Order "Jedi Order")[[52]](#cite_note-SW9-52) who shared their name with a [red-skinned species](/wiki/Sith_(species) "Sith (species)").[[53]](#cite_note-3rd_Grade_and_Writing-53) Established by a [rogue Jedi](/wiki/Unidentified_rogue_Jedi "Unidentified rogue Jedi") during the [Hundred-Year Darkness](/wiki/Hundred-Year_Darkness "Hundred-Year Darkness"), the Sith sought further knowledge and power through learning the dark side of the Force. Eventually, this [Jedi](/wiki/Jedi "Jedi") was able to amass a [Jedi splinter group](/wiki/Jedi_splinter_group "Jedi splinter group") with a sizable following, all of whom adhered to this new philosophy that embraced the dark side.[[40]](#cite_note-Sith-40) This schism in the Jedi Order led to a civil war where the Jedi and the newly-founded Sith Order, once brothers and sisters in the Force, fought against one another for power.[[52]](#cite_note-SW9-52) The war ended in the defeat of the Sith, who fled from known [space](/wiki/Realspace "Realspace"). Unbeknownst to the Jedi, however, the Sith settled on [Korriban](/wiki/Moraband "Moraband"), a [world](/wiki/Planet "Planet") of [red](/wiki/Color "Color") sands that was later known as Moraband, where they rebuilt in secret and waited for another chance to strike.[[40]](#cite_note-Sith-40)

#### Exile on Korriban[]

:   "*Known long ago as Korriban, this ancient homeworld of the Sith was abandoned after countless wars transformed it into an infertile wasteland.*"
:   ―Darth Sidious[[28]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Sith-28)

 [![Sith temples and monuments were constructed on Korriban during the time of the ancient Sith.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/20/Valley_of_the_Dark_Lords_TCW.png/revision/latest?cb=20200224012406) [![Sith temples and monuments were constructed on Korriban during the time of the ancient Sith.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/20/Valley_of_the_Dark_Lords_TCW.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200224012406)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/20/Valley_of_the_Dark_Lords_TCW.png/revision/latest?cb=20200224012406) 

Sith temples and monuments were constructed on Korriban during the time of the ancient Sith.

 

As the Sith Order grew, they constructed massive [temples](/wiki/Sith_temple "Sith temple") and tombs on Korriban in a location known as the [Valley of the Dark Lords](/wiki/Valley_of_the_Dark_Lords "Valley of the Dark Lords").[[17]](#cite_note-Sacrifice-17) The Sith built [empires](/wiki/Sith_Empire "Sith Empire") on the backs of their [slaves](/wiki/Slavery "Slavery")[[9]](#cite_note-EfK-9) and fought wars against the Jedi for control of the galaxy. During these wars, they built massive [superweapons](/wiki/Superweapon "Superweapon") powered by giant [kyber crystals](/wiki/Kyber_crystal "Kyber crystal").[[54]](#cite_note-The_Big_Bang-54)[[55]](#cite_note-Death_Star_Superlaser-55) Eventually, a trade route in the [Outer Rim](/wiki/Outer_Rim_Territories "Outer Rim Territories") came to be known as the [Cloak of the Sith](/wiki/Cloak_of_the_Sith "Cloak of the Sith"), a name which[[56]](#cite_note-Smuggler's_Guide-56) was similar to how Sith Lords were known to wear dark cloaks.[[43]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-43)

#### War on the Old Republic[]

:   "*The Sith Order grew, spreading its might across the galaxy.*"
:   ―Darth Sidious[[28]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Sith-28)

 [![The Sith encountered and later betrayed the Drengir.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/ba/TrappedDrengir-2021THR4.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210409022355) [![The Sith encountered and later betrayed the Drengir.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/ba/TrappedDrengir-2021THR4.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20210409022355)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/ba/TrappedDrengir-2021THR4.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20210409022355) 

The Sith encountered and later betrayed the Drengir.

 

It was believed the [lightfoil](/wiki/Lightfoil "Lightfoil") was made by the early Sith.[[57]](#cite_note-Knights_of_Fate-57) The Sith also formed an alliance with the [Nightsisters](/wiki/Nightsisters "Nightsisters") of [Dathomir](/wiki/Dathomir "Dathomir") at some point, but the "old alliance," as they came to dub it, eventually ceased. Ultimately, the Nightsisters would decide to only retain loyalty to each other.[[58]](#cite_note-Monster-58) Around [2500 BBY](/wiki/2500_BBY "2500 BBY"), the Sith allied with the [Drengir](/wiki/Drengir "Drengir"), and for a [time](/wiki/Time "Time") they worked alongside each other, until around the same year[[39]](#cite_note-Timelines-39) they betrayed the living plants.[[59]](#cite_note-The_High_Republic_(2021)_4-59) The Sith [left the Drengir](/wiki/Capture_of_the_Drengir "Capture of the Drengir") locked on the [Amaxine space station](/wiki/Amaxine_Space_Station "Amaxine Space Station") via the [binding statues](/wiki/Binding_statues "Binding statues").[[60]](#cite_note-ItD-60)

[Exim Panshard](/wiki/Exim_Panshard "Exim Panshard") was a Sith [viceroy](/wiki/Viceroy "Viceroy") who ruled over a [forgotten planet](/wiki/Unidentified_planet_(Exim_Panshard) "Unidentified planet (Exim Panshard)") in a bloody rule, culminating in the creation of a [mask](/wiki/Mask_of_Viceroy_Exim_Panshard "Mask of Viceroy Exim Panshard") that, fueled by the deaths of countless civilians, he cling onto life within.[[26]](#cite_note-Shadow_of_the_Sith-26)

 [![The Jedi and Sith waged a series of wars throughout their history so ruinous that at points each was brought to the brink of destruction.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/87/GreatSithWarsBas-Relief-SW100Objects.png/revision/latest?cb=20230419025101) [![The Jedi and Sith waged a series of wars throughout their history so ruinous that at points each was brought to the brink of destruction.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/87/GreatSithWarsBas-Relief-SW100Objects.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/300?cb=20230419025101)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/87/GreatSithWarsBas-Relief-SW100Objects.png/revision/latest?cb=20230419025101) 

The Jedi and Sith waged a series of wars throughout their history so ruinous that at points each was brought to the brink of destruction.

 

At one point, nearly five thousand [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") before the [rise](/wiki/Proclamation_of_the_New_Order "Proclamation of the New Order") of the [Galactic Empire](/wiki/Galactic_Empire "Galactic Empire"), the Sith waged a [war](/wiki/Sith_war_(Old_Republic) "Sith war (Old Republic)") against the Jedi and the Old Republic. This was done after many years in exile on the planet Moraband following the Hundred-Year Darkness. During this war, the Sith [attacked](/wiki/Battle_of_Coruscant_(Sith_war) "Battle of Coruscant (Sith war)") the Republic capital [Coruscant](/wiki/Coruscant "Coruscant").[[19]](#cite_note-CL2016-19) This allowed the Sith to build a [shrine](/wiki/Shrine_in_the_Depths "Shrine in the Depths") on the planet, which became a place of immense dark side power. Eventually, the Jedi were able to repel the Sith from Coruscant. The Jedi raised their own [temple](/wiki/Imperial_Palace "Imperial Palace") over the Coruscant shrine in an attempt to contain and eliminate its power.[[18]](#cite_note-Tarkin-18)

Around this time, the Jedi and Sith engaged in a number of battles and wars like the [Great Hyperspace War](/wiki/Great_Hyperspace_War "Great Hyperspace War")[[7]](#cite_note-Nexus-7) and the [Great Sith Wars](/wiki/Great_Sith_Wars "Great Sith Wars").[[61]](#cite_note-sw100-61) The [Massassi](/wiki/Massassi "Massassi"), a [slave](/wiki/Slavery "Slavery") [race](/wiki/Species "Species") controlled by the Sith, constructed the [Great Temple](/wiki/Great_Temple "Great Temple") on [Yavin 4](/wiki/Yavin_4 "Yavin 4"), allegedly under the leadership of the Sith [Lord](/wiki/Lord "Lord") [Naga Sadow](/wiki/Naga_Sadow "Naga Sadow").[[62]](#cite_note-Ultimate_Star_Wars-62)[[63]](#cite_note-BTM-63)

#### A bastion of the Sith[]

:   "*It was here on… on this dead world… that the Jedi struck a terrible blow against the Sith. Many of our order were struck down. All because they wanted to be* free*.*"
:   ―Darth Sidious, to Darth Maul[[64]](#cite_note-Darth_Maul_(2017)_2-64)

 [![Jedi and Sith both perished when Malachor was scourged by the power within an ancient Sith temple.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/06/GreatScourgeofMalachor-TotA1.png/revision/latest?cb=20201027144205) [![Jedi and Sith both perished when Malachor was scourged by the power within an ancient Sith temple.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/06/GreatScourgeofMalachor-TotA1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20201027144205)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/06/GreatScourgeofMalachor-TotA1.png/revision/latest?cb=20201027144205) 

Jedi and Sith both perished when Malachor was scourged by the power within an ancient Sith temple.

 

The Sith continued to expand their empire erecting temples on multiple planets. One such [temple](/wiki/Malachor_Sith_Temple "Malachor Sith Temple") was built on the world [Malachor](/wiki/Malachor "Malachor"). At the heart of this temple was a [superweapon](/wiki/Malachor_superweapon "Malachor superweapon") powered by a giant kyber crystal. The Jedi eventually learned of the weapon and assaulted the temple. A savage [battle](/wiki/Great_Scourge_of_Malachor "Great Scourge of Malachor") was then waged between the Sith Empire and the invading Jedi Knights. During the battle, the temple was activated, petrifying everyone on the planet. This would result in the planet being forbidden from Jedi and becoming a legend for millennia to come.[[20]](#cite_note-Twilight-20)

#### Resurgence of the Sith[]

Over the course of thousands of years, the rivalry between the Sith and Jedi took many forms.[[65]](#cite_note-Insider230-65) The Sith [resurged](/wiki/Resurgence_of_the_Sith "Resurgence of the Sith") in one conflict that became very desperate, which was likely why the Jedi Order turned to [Form VII](/wiki/Form_VII "Form VII") "Juyo." That aggressive lightsaber combat form, however, resulted in a number of Jedi falling to the dark side. After the conflict had finished, the Jedi banned its study.[[57]](#cite_note-Knights_of_Fate-57)

#### Conflict for the Force[]

:   "*The Jedi and Sith battled each other over countless generations.*"
:   ―Luke Skywalker[[66]](#cite_note-Star_Wars:_The_Secrets_of_the_Jedi-66)

 [![The Darkseekers were Sith tasked with hunting and eliminating threats to their order's rule over the galaxy.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4a/Darkseekers-2020DoctorAphra24.png/revision/latest?cb=20240117015814) [![The Darkseekers were Sith tasked with hunting and eliminating threats to their order's rule over the galaxy.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4a/Darkseekers-2020DoctorAphra24.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20240117015814)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4a/Darkseekers-2020DoctorAphra24.png/revision/latest?cb=20240117015814) 

The Darkseekers were Sith tasked with hunting and eliminating threats to their order's rule over the galaxy.

 

At one time, the Sith established an [oppressive rule](/wiki/Era_of_the_Sith "Era of the Sith") over the galaxy.[[24]](#cite_note-Episode_III-24) During the reign of the Sith, a cult named the [Ascendant](/wiki/Ascendant "Ascendant") flourished[[67]](#cite_note-Aphra_(2020)_20-67) and attempted to recreate the powers of the Force with technological innovations. However, the cult was an enemy of the Sith[[68]](#cite_note-Aphra_(2020)_22-68) and hunted by its [Darkseekers](/wiki/Darkseekers "Darkseekers"), who regarded the Ascendant as an order of heretics. Although Ascendant leader [Miril](/wiki/Miril "Miril") was once able to escape a team of Darkseekers in the [Floating Catacombs](/wiki/Floating_Catacombs "Floating Catacombs"),[[6]](#cite_note-Aphra_(2020)_24-6) the Sith eventually located the Ascendant's [primary temple](/wiki/Tomb_of_the_Spark_Eternal "Tomb of the Spark Eternal") on [Bar'leth](/wiki/Bar%27leth "Bar'leth") and [attacked](/wiki/Slaughter_of_the_Ascendant "Slaughter of the Ascendant")[[68]](#cite_note-Aphra_(2020)_22-68) while the Ascendant worked on finishing the [Spark Eternal](/wiki/Spark_Eternal "Spark Eternal").[[6]](#cite_note-Aphra_(2020)_24-6) As her fellow cultists were cut down, Miril gave her life to hide the Spark away to prevent it from being recovered by the Sith.[[68]](#cite_note-Aphra_(2020)_22-68)

During one conflict, the Jedi and Sith [fought](/wiki/Battle_of_Takodana_(Jedi_versus_Sith) "Battle of Takodana (Jedi versus Sith)") on the planet [Takodana](/wiki/Takodana "Takodana"). The [pirate](/wiki/Pirate "Pirate") [Maz Kanata](/wiki/Maz_Kanata "Maz Kanata") later built her [castle](/wiki/Takodana_Castle "Takodana Castle") on top of the legendary battlefield.[[69]](#cite_note-TFA_VD-69) [Jedi Master](/wiki/Jedi_Master "Jedi Master") [Tal Bota](/wiki/Tal_Bota "Tal Bota") was a legendary Jedi who often fought against the Sith. His life became the inspiration for holostories, one of which depicted him fighting many Sith troops at once.[[70]](#cite_note-HRA_6-70) The legendary Sith [Darth Wrend](/wiki/Darth_Wrend "Darth Wrend") fought against the Jedi. Despite being believed dead, Wrend returned to continue to battle.[[71]](#cite_note-Master_&_Apprentice-71) At some point, the Jedi [Radaki](/wiki/Darth_Krall "Darth Krall") fell to the dark side, becoming the Sith Darth Krall and winning the [Battle of Wasted Years](/wiki/Battle_of_Wasted_Years "Battle of Wasted Years"). He also tamed the [Nightmare Conjunction](/wiki/Nightmare_Conjunction "Nightmare Conjunction")[[72]](#cite_note-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost-72) and wielded a lightsaber with a gold [hilt](/wiki/Lightsaber_hilt "Lightsaber hilt").[[73]](#cite_note-High_Republic_7-73)

#### The rise and fall of Darth Momin[]

:   "*With resources inherited from Lady Shaa and the help of acolytes desperate to aid me in my work, I designed a great engine. It was a weapon, of course, powerful enough to burn the city to ash.*"
:   ―Darth Momin, to Darth Vader[[14]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith_22-14)

 [![Darth Momin venerated the power of the dark side of the Force.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/21/MominActivatesWeapon-2017DarthVader22.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190601202246) [![Darth Momin venerated the power of the dark side of the Force.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/21/MominActivatesWeapon-2017DarthVader22.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20190601202246)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/21/MominActivatesWeapon-2017DarthVader22.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20190601202246) 

Darth Momin venerated the power of the dark side of the Force.

 

The Sith Lord [Darth Momin](/wiki/Darth_Momin "Darth Momin"), after killing his Master [Darth Shaa](/wiki/Darth_Shaa "Darth Shaa"), sought more knowledge in the dark side. He decided that his only audience was the Force and yearned to be worthy of it. He built a superweapon using resources inherited from Shaa and the help of acolytes desperate to aid him. [Darth Momin's superweapon](/wiki/Darth_Momin%27s_superweapon "Darth Momin's superweapon") had the power to incinerate an entire city, but his true plan was different. He wanted to pour the Force into the weapon's engine and freeze the terrified expressions of the people in time forever, creating an artwork depicting fear and pain devoted to the dark side of the Force. When he [attempted](/wiki/Darth_Momin%27s_destruction_of_a_city "Darth Momin's destruction of a city") this, the Jedi intervened and Momin's body was destroyed, yet his mind remained inside his [mask](/wiki/Mask_of_Lord_Momin "Mask of Lord Momin") where he waited for his revival as ages passed.[[14]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith_22-14)

In the meantime, however, the Sith buried knowledge of Momin and his ideas on the belief that he had been a heretic. The Sith refused to recount information about Momin into their holocrons. The Jedi, too, made no mention of the Sith Lord in their holocrons[[36]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_21-36) and locked his mask away.[[74]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_8-74) Nonetheless, the Sith at some point used[[75]](#cite_note-Dark_Droids_1-75) Momin's [Fermata Cage](/wiki/Fermata_Cage "Fermata Cage")[[76]](#cite_note-HE_2-76) to lock away a [droid intelligence](/wiki/Unidentified_droid_(Fermata_Cage) "Unidentified droid (Fermata Cage)").[[75]](#cite_note-Dark_Droids_1-75) The Fermata Cage was then hidden within a [dark side hellscape](/wiki/Dark_side_hellscape "Dark side hellscape")[[77]](#cite_note-Crimson_Reign_5-77) Momin knew of.[[14]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith_22-14)

#### The Dark Age[]

:   "*After thousands of years of war, the Sith were pushed to the edge of extinction.*"
:   ―Darth Sidious[[28]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Sith-28)

During a period of time known as the [Dark Age](/wiki/Fall_of_the_Old_Republic "Fall of the Old Republic"), the [Jedi-Sith War](/wiki/Jedi-Sith_War "Jedi-Sith War") broke out. Early on in the war, the Sith [attacked](/wiki/Battle_of_Coruscant_(Jedi-Sith_War) "Battle of Coruscant (Jedi-Sith War)") the Old Republic capital world of Coruscant. The Sith successfully captured the planet as well as the Jedi Temple. The [Liberation of Coruscant](/wiki/Liberation_of_Coruscant "Liberation of Coruscant") was one of the last battles of the Jedi-Sith War and resulted in the Sith being driven from Coruscant.[[78]](#cite_note-SWP-78)

#### Destruction and rebirth[]

:   "*A long, long time ago, there were many Sith. We rose up against the simpering light…we warred with the Jedi…and lost as we also warred amongst our own kind.*"
:   ―Darth Sidious, to Darth Vader[[79]](#cite_note-Darth_Vader_20-79)

 [![The Sith were reformed by Darth Bane, who decreed that only two Sith Lords could exist at any given time: a master and an apprentice.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3d/DarthBane-2020DarthVader27variant.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20250413045912) [![The Sith were reformed by Darth Bane, who decreed that only two Sith Lords could exist at any given time: a master and an apprentice.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3d/DarthBane-2020DarthVader27variant.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20250413045912)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3d/DarthBane-2020DarthVader27variant.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20250413045912) 

The Sith were reformed by Darth Bane, who decreed that only two Sith Lords could exist at any given time: a master and an apprentice.

 

The Sith numbered thousands, yet they were eventually[[80]](#cite_note-Fun_Facts-80) [defeated](/wiki/Defeat_of_the_Sith "Defeat of the Sith") at[[41]](#cite_note-Helmet_Collection_29-41) the world[[38]](#cite_note-VE-38) of [Ruusan](/wiki/Ruusan "Ruusan")[[41]](#cite_note-Helmet_Collection_29-41) in the [Mid Rim Territories](/wiki/Mid_Rim_Territories "Mid Rim Territories").[[38]](#cite_note-VE-38) Despite the [Sith armada](/wiki/Sith_armada "Sith armada")'s quantitative advantage over the much smaller [Ghostfinder fleet](/wiki/Ghostfinder_fleet "Ghostfinder fleet"), the Sith were outmatched.[[8]](#cite_note-EE-8) The Sith's quest to gain power was ultimately their undoing, as the dark side made them turn against one another. Within a year, the Jedi managed to defeat the infighting Sith, bringing what was left of the dark order to its knees. However, one Sith, [Darth Bane](/wiki/Darth_Bane "Darth Bane"), survived. With his fellow Sith Lords destroyed, he reformed the order by establishing the Rule of Two, mandating that only two Sith, a master and an apprentice, could exist at any given time, lest they fall prey to infighting.[[17]](#cite_note-Sacrifice-17) To keep Bane's philosophy alive, the apprentice needed to slay their master and take on an apprentice of their own, or the master could train another apprentice and have them kill and replace their current apprentice. Bane had also initiated a revenge plot against the Jedi, called the [Grand Plan](/wiki/Grand_Plan "Grand Plan").[[24]](#cite_note-Episode_III-24)

The Sith abandoned their traditional [homeworld](/wiki/Homeworld "Homeworld") of Moraband after it was scarred by many wars.[[81]](#cite_note-datamora-81) Eventually, [Darth](/wiki/Darth "Darth") Bane was [killed](/wiki/Death "Death") and was [buried](/wiki/Tomb_of_Darth_Bane "Tomb of Darth Bane") in the Valley of the Dark Lords on its surface,[[17]](#cite_note-Sacrifice-17) but the Rule of Two continued through his apprentice, [Darth Zannah](/wiki/Darth_Zannah "Darth Zannah"). It was rumored that Zannah had killed Bane on the [Inner Rim](/wiki/Inner_Rim_Territories "Inner Rim Territories") [planet](/wiki/Planet "Planet") of [Ambria](/wiki/Ambria "Ambria").[[82]](#cite_note-HC_2-82) The Jedi believed that they had destroyed Bane's rule and,[[83]](#cite_note-SW_2020_20-83) incorrectly thinking the Sith extinct,[[2]](#cite_note-Episode_I-2) entered into a golden age[[83]](#cite_note-SW_2020_20-83) remembered as the [High Republic Era](/wiki/High_Republic_Era "High Republic Era").[[84]](#cite_note-Kylo_2-84) Many Sith worlds were also quarantined, including [Rhelg](/wiki/Rhelg "Rhelg"), [Jaguada](/wiki/Jaguada "Jaguada"), and [Ziost](/wiki/Ziost "Ziost"). Some worlds were so cleansed of their Sith history that even locals had no idea of their past.[[4]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-4) The [Lerct Historical Institute](/wiki/Lerct_Historical_Institute "Lerct Historical Institute") forbade research into the Sith as something arcane and occult that had no place among its work.[[26]](#cite_note-Shadow_of_the_Sith-26)

### In the shadows[]

#### High Republic Era[]

##### Threat of the Nameless[]

:   "*This act was a* gift*, to everyone who touches the Force. Jedi, Sith,* all of us*.*"
:   ―Azlin Rell, to Yoda[[85]](#cite_note-SOS_1-85)

 [![The fallen Jedi Azlin Rell invoked the name of the Sith when justifying the destruction of an entire city on Travyx Prime as a gift to all Force-sensitives.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/24/AllOfUs-THRSOS1.png/revision/latest?cb=20240626035624) [![The fallen Jedi Azlin Rell invoked the name of the Sith when justifying the destruction of an entire city on Travyx Prime as a gift to all Force-sensitives.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/24/AllOfUs-THRSOS1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20240626035624)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/24/AllOfUs-THRSOS1.png/revision/latest?cb=20240626035624) 

The fallen Jedi Azlin Rell invoked the name of the Sith when justifying the destruction of an entire city on Travyx Prime as a gift to all Force-sensitives.

 

The Sith stayed in hiding for a thousand years, their survival unknown to the Jedi, as they continued their revenge against the Jedi through Bane's Grand Plan. With Sith teachings passed down by Bane's Rule of Two, the Order managed to survive.[[17]](#cite_note-Sacrifice-17) During the High Republic Era, the [Nameless](/wiki/Shrikarai "Shrikarai") beings emerged as a major threat to any individual sensitive to the Force. Former Jedi [Azlin Rell](/wiki/Azlin_Rell "Azlin Rell")—who fell to the dark side out of his fear and lost his mind—resolved to wipe out the entire species, reasoning that such would be a gift to every Force-sensitive in the galaxy, including the Sith. While he made it clear to the Jedi High Council that he was not their enemy because he was no Sith, Rell ensured a city on the world [Travyx Prime](/wiki/Travyx_Prime "Travyx Prime") was [destroyed](/wiki/Attack_on_Travyx_Prime "Attack on Travyx Prime"), thereby silencing a possible lead to the Nameless homeworld, [Planet X](/wiki/Sophros "Sophros"). He proclaimed to Yoda his actions were a gift to every Force user, including the Jedi and Sith,[[85]](#cite_note-SOS_1-85) but Yoda did not take his words as proof of the Sith Order's return.[[2]](#cite_note-Episode_I-2)

##### The Stranger[]

###### Masters of shadows[]

:   "*What are you?*"  
    "*I have no name. But the Jedi like you might call me… Sith.*"
:   ―Sol and the Stranger[[86]](#cite_note-Night-86)

 [![The Stranger, also known as "the Master," was a mysterious Sith who sought to train an acolyte.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f4/TheStrangerPushes-Day.png/revision/latest?cb=20240627144422) [![The Stranger, also known as "the Master," was a mysterious Sith who sought to train an acolyte.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f4/TheStrangerPushes-Day.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20240627144422)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f4/TheStrangerPushes-Day.png/revision/latest?cb=20240627144422) 

The Stranger, also known as "the Master," was a mysterious Sith who sought to train an acolyte.

 

By the later period of the High Republic Era,[[87]](#cite_note-The_Acolyte-87) a [Dark Lord of the Sith](/wiki/Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith "Dark Lord of the Sith") named [Darth Plagueis](/wiki/Darth_Plagueis "Darth Plagueis")[[24]](#cite_note-Episode_III-24) was active.[[87]](#cite_note-The_Acolyte-87) Furthermore, a [human Jedi](/wiki/The_Stranger "The Stranger")[[88]](#cite_note-Teach_/_Corrupt-88) trained by Jedi Master [Vernestra Rwoh](/wiki/Vernestra_Rwoh "Vernestra Rwoh")[[87]](#cite_note-The_Acolyte-87) fell to the dark side of the Force[[86]](#cite_note-Night-86) and abandoned the Jedi Order, keeping himself out of Rwoh's reach.[[87]](#cite_note-The_Acolyte-87) The individual, who claimed to have no name[[86]](#cite_note-Night-86) and thus became known as "the Stranger,"[[89]](#cite_note-Qimir_DB-89) became a Sith[[90]](#cite_note-Stunts-90) as the apprentice to Plagueis.[[91]](#cite_note-Leslye_EW-91)

The Stranger also operated[[86]](#cite_note-Night-86) publicly as the [merchant](/wiki/Merchant "Merchant")[[92]](#cite_note-Revenge_Justice-92) Qimir.[[86]](#cite_note-Night-86) The Stranger kept his identity well-hidden[[92]](#cite_note-Revenge_Justice-92) and sought to see the dream of the Jedi Order overthrown.[[93]](#cite_note-Lost_/_Found-93) It was his ultimate hope to wield his power however he wished.[[86]](#cite_note-Night-86) A location also known to Plagueis,[[87]](#cite_note-The_Acolyte-87) he based himself within an [island](/wiki/The_Stranger%27s_island "The Stranger's island") [cave](/wiki/The_Stranger%27s_cave "The Stranger's cave") located on[[94]](#cite_note-Cave_Stranger-94) the planet[[95]](#cite_note-AcolyteVG-95) [Bal'demnic](/wiki/Bal%27demnic "Bal'demnic"),[[96]](#cite_note-Fry-96) where he could operate without the knowledge of the Jedi.[[94]](#cite_note-Cave_Stranger-94) Plagueis took to lurking[[97]](#cite_note-Acolyte_Companion-97) in the shadows around the Stranger's dwelling. Combined with the Stranger's reluctance to call himself a Sith, the dark side user's true loyalties thus remained elusive, especially as they related to Plagueis.[[98]](#cite_note-229POV-98)

###### Searching for an acolyte[]

:   "*What do you want?*"  
    "*Freedom. The freedom to wield my power the way I like. Without having to answer to Jedi like you. I want a pupil, an Acolyte.*"
:   ―Sol and the Stranger[[86]](#cite_note-Night-86)

 [![Mae-ho Aniseya was trained as an acolyte and Sith assassin by the Stranger.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f6/RevengeJusticeThumbnailAcolyte.png/revision/latest?cb=20240606044151) [![Mae-ho Aniseya was trained as an acolyte and Sith assassin by the Stranger.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f6/RevengeJusticeThumbnailAcolyte.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20240606044151)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/f6/RevengeJusticeThumbnailAcolyte.png/revision/latest?cb=20240606044151) 

Mae-ho Aniseya was trained as an acolyte and Sith assassin by the Stranger.

 

In time, the Stranger sought out a disciple to train[[86]](#cite_note-Night-86) despite the Rule of Two:[[17]](#cite_note-Sacrifice-17) his decision was to train a Sith acolyte,[[86]](#cite_note-Night-86) a position that, in theory, would exist outside the rule.[[51]](#cite_note-Nightsisters-51) He eventually discovered a human woman named [Mae-ho Aniseya](/wiki/Mae-ho_Aniseya "Mae-ho Aniseya"), who in childhood had been part of a [witch coven](/wiki/Brendok_coven "Brendok coven") alongside her twin sister [Verosha Aniseya](/wiki/Verosha_Aniseya "Verosha Aniseya") until an [incident involving the Jedi Order](/wiki/Mission_to_Brendok "Mission to Brendok")[[99]](#cite_note-Destiny_Acolyte-99) in [148 BBY](/wiki/148_BBY "148 BBY").[[100]](#cite_note-148_Date-100) With the Sith keeping his identity a secret,[[86]](#cite_note-Night-86) Mae swore herself to and began to be trained by the individual, whom she knew only as "the Master,"[[92]](#cite_note-Revenge_Justice-92) out of a desire to have revenge on the [four Jedi involved in the Brendok mission](/wiki/Brendok_four "Brendok four"), among them Jedi Master [Sol](/wiki/Sol "Sol"), who had slain her mother [Aniseya](/wiki/Aniseya "Aniseya")[[87]](#cite_note-The_Acolyte-87) out of a misunderstanding and then covered up his actions.[[101]](#cite_note-Choice-101) Ultimately, Mae sought to please "the Master"[[92]](#cite_note-Revenge_Justice-92) but feared the man as well.[[102]](#cite_note-Day-102) Under his public cover,[[86]](#cite_note-Night-86) "Qimir" worked with Mae as a trader of rare goods[[92]](#cite_note-Revenge_Justice-92) and fellow servant of the Master,[[102]](#cite_note-Day-102) with Mae unaware he was none-other-than her mentor.[[86]](#cite_note-Night-86) The Master further, in the words of his Qimir persona, "collected" people, which was "Qimir's" cover story.[[102]](#cite_note-Day-102)

 [![The Stranger killed several Jedi in order to ensure that his identity as a Sith remained concealed.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/83/QimirLightsabers-Night.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20240703043124) [![The Stranger killed several Jedi in order to ensure that his identity as a Sith remained concealed.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/83/QimirLightsabers-Night.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20240703043124)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/8/83/QimirLightsabers-Night.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20240703043124) 

The Stranger killed several Jedi in order to ensure that his identity as a Sith remained concealed.

 

Under the Master's tutelage,[[92]](#cite_note-Revenge_Justice-92) Mae served as a [Sith assassin](/wiki/Sith_assassin "Sith assassin")[[103]](#cite_note-114_Interview-103) and acolyte.[[86]](#cite_note-Night-86) Eventually, he demanded she slay a Jedi without a weapon as her final test. As per his wishes, Mae began a [quest](/wiki/Mae%27s_quest "Mae's quest") to kill the four Jedi involved in her past, Masters Sol, [Torbin](/wiki/Torbin "Torbin"), [Indara](/wiki/Indara "Indara"), and [Kelnacca](/wiki/Kelnacca "Kelnacca"),[[92]](#cite_note-Revenge_Justice-92) in [132 BBY](/wiki/132_BBY "132 BBY").[[100]](#cite_note-148_Date-100) After the deaths of Indara and Torbin, with the former killed at her own hand with a knife but the latter having taken his own life when confronted by Mae, Mae learned that her sister was in fact alive,[[92]](#cite_note-Revenge_Justice-92) which ultimately convinced her to abandon her life as the Master's servant during her [mission to slay Kelnacca](/wiki/Mission_to_Khofar "Mission to Khofar"). Unknown to Mae, the Master himself had arrived[[102]](#cite_note-Day-102)—as he was none-other-than Qimir,[[86]](#cite_note-Night-86) who she betrayed and left "trapped" in the woods—and would kill Kelnacca himself. Afterward, he engaged a grouping of Jedi under Sol who had journeyed to [Kelnacca's shelter](/wiki/Kelnacca%27s_shelter "Kelnacca's shelter"),[[102]](#cite_note-Day-102) slaughtering all but Sol over the course of the battle. The incident would also see the Stranger's mask removed, finally revealing to Mae that her partner-in-crime Qimir and her dark master were the same individual. The Stranger further revealed himself as a Sith to Sol.[[86]](#cite_note-Night-86)

###### Stranger no more[]

:   "*I need you to help me find someone.*"  
    "*Who?*"  
    "*A pupil of mine before he turned to evil.*"
:   ―Vernestra Rwoh and Mae-ho Aniseya[[87]](#cite_note-The_Acolyte-87)

 [![Mae-ho Aniseya had fallen out with the Stranger, who directed his attention to her twin sister, Verosha Aniseya.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/aa/QimirPointIsland-TeachCorrupt.png/revision/latest?cb=20240703143841) [![Mae-ho Aniseya had fallen out with the Stranger, who directed his attention to her twin sister, Verosha Aniseya.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/aa/QimirPointIsland-TeachCorrupt.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20240703143841)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/aa/QimirPointIsland-TeachCorrupt.png/revision/latest?cb=20240703143841) 

Mae-ho Aniseya had fallen out with the Stranger, who directed his attention to her twin sister, Verosha Aniseya.

 

After Qimir's double identity was revealed and the Sith was swarmed by a grouping of [umbramoths](/wiki/Umbramoth "Umbramoth"), Mae knocked out her sister and swapped places with her, returning to the Jedi transport with Sol. Meanwhile, the Stranger reclaimed his mask and cloak before finding the unconscious Osha,[[86]](#cite_note-Night-86) who he brought back with him to the unknown world where the Stranger had based himself. Waking up in the Stranger's custody, Osha followed him as the man went out to take a swim and claimed his lightsaber, unaware that he was aware of her actions. Noticing how she thought killing an unarmed foe was not honorable, the Stranger managed to convince her into letting him live and divulged details of his past, attempting to tempt Osha into doubting the ideals of the Jedi and instead embrace his own. All the while, Sol discovered that Mae had swapped places with her sister and subdued her, leaving the orbit of Khofar and promising to save Osha from Mae's master once they had a chance to truly talk.[[88]](#cite_note-Teach_/_Corrupt-88)

Just as Sol departed, a Jedi investigation team under Master Vernestra Rwoh arrived on Khofar, where they discovered the aftermath of the battle with the Stranger. Unaware of who had committed the massacre, Padawan [Mog Adana](/wiki/Mog_Adana "Mog Adana") suggested that Sol had fallen to the dark side.[[88]](#cite_note-Teach_/_Corrupt-88) With all parties converging on Brendok once Sol returned to the world where all his troubles had began, as Sol activated his tracking beacon for the Jedi to follow him and Osha experienced a Force vision of his death on the planet, Sol and the Stranger began a [final duel](/wiki/Duel_on_Brendok "Duel on Brendok"), after which Mae rejected the ways of anger and instead wanted to see Sol brought to justice for his crime: striking down her mother and lying about his actions. However, the revelation that her master had killed her mother broke Osha, who Force choked the Jedi Master—thereby killing a Jedi without a weapon—and bled his lightsaber.[[87]](#cite_note-The_Acolyte-87)

 [![Verosha Aniseya turned to the dark side and replaced her sister as the Stranger's new acolyte.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/76/MasterAndAcolyte-TheAcolyte.png/revision/latest?cb=20240729235734) [![Verosha Aniseya turned to the dark side and replaced her sister as the Stranger's new acolyte.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/76/MasterAndAcolyte-TheAcolyte.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20240729235734)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/76/MasterAndAcolyte-TheAcolyte.png/revision/latest?cb=20240729235734) 

Verosha Aniseya turned to the dark side and replaced her sister as the Stranger's new acolyte.

 

Osha accepted the station as the Stranger's acolyte, while Mae allowed her memory of her sister to be wiped so she could be handed over to the Jedi. As the Jedi party under Rwoh arrived too late to catch the Stranger, Rwoh blamed the murders of Kelnecca, Indara, and Torbin on Sol. Having sensed her former disciple's presence, however, she met with Mae and requested her aid in finding the Stranger. Meanwhile, Osha returned to the Stranger's island with him as his new acolyte,[[87]](#cite_note-The_Acolyte-87) all while Plagueis continued to lurk on the planet.[[97]](#cite_note-Acolyte_Companion-97)

#### Late Republic Era[]

:   "*For a thousand years we have kept to the shadows, not afraid of the Jedi—but* ourselves*. The dark side is powerful. It is* too *powerful. The weak will meekly stand in regimented order. The Sith… One master. One apprentice. No more. For generations. Generations building to* me*.*"
:   ―Darth Sidious, to Darth Vader[[79]](#cite_note-Darth_Vader_20-79)

 [![The Sith remained hidden for a millennium, allowing the Jedi to believe that their ancient nemesis had gone extinct.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d6/Acolyte-Thereheis.png/revision/latest?cb=20250203031752) [![The Sith remained hidden for a millennium, allowing the Jedi to believe that their ancient nemesis had gone extinct.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d6/Acolyte-Thereheis.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20250203031752)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d6/Acolyte-Thereheis.png/revision/latest?cb=20250203031752) 

The Sith remained hidden for a millennium, allowing the Jedi to believe that their ancient nemesis had gone extinct.

 

In [82 BBY](/wiki/82_BBY "82 BBY"),[[104]](#cite_note-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost_Date-104) the Jedi [Padawan](/wiki/Padawan "Padawan") [Dooku](/wiki/Dooku "Dooku"), after [encountering](/wiki/Mission_to_Asusto "Mission to Asusto") the [Presagers of Hakotei](/wiki/Presagers_of_Hakotei "Presagers of Hakotei") cult, heard the voice of[[105]](#cite_note-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost_script-105) the Sith Lord[[106]](#cite_note-Sith_Lord-106) [Darth Skrye](/wiki/Darth_Skrye "Darth Skrye") in a [Force vision](/wiki/Force_vision "Force vision"). Within the vision of a possible future, Skrye stated that the Sith were reborn and that something called the [Cauldron](/wiki/Cauldron "Cauldron") was opening, all alongside the sound of a planet being torn in two and an explosion. The visions greatly worried Dooku, who also saw a glimpse of himself falling to the dark side as the apprentice of another Sith Lord, but Jedi Master [Lene Kostana](/wiki/Lene_Kostana "Lene Kostana") tried to ease Dooku's concern by assuring him what he saw were merely possibilities, not certain futures.[[105]](#cite_note-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost_script-105)

Eventually, the Sith apprentice known as Darth Sidious[[18]](#cite_note-Tarkin-18)—the same Sith glimpsed by Dooku in his vision[[105]](#cite_note-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost_script-105)—betrayed his master Darth Plagueis, by killing him in his [sleep](/wiki/Sleep "Sleep"), seizing the status of master for himself as he forwards a plot to destroy the Jedi.[[24]](#cite_note-Episode_III-24) Thus, generations after the fall of the Sith,[[79]](#cite_note-Darth_Vader_20-79) Sidious moved to strike a fatal blow against the Jedi Order and the [Galactic Republic](/wiki/Galactic_Republic "Galactic Republic").[[24]](#cite_note-Episode_III-24) Orchestrating his public persona's rise to the Republic's [Chancellorship](/wiki/Office_of_the_Chancellor "Office of the Chancellor")[[2]](#cite_note-Episode_I-2) and the creation of an army that would purge the Jedi, Darth Sidious fulfilled the return of Sith rule over the galaxy, giving rise to the [New Order](/wiki/New_Order "New Order") under himself as Emperor.[[24]](#cite_note-Episode_III-24)

### Fall of the Galactic Republic[]

#### The Phantom Menace[]

:   "*They have numbers on their side. And the faith of the Republic.*"  
    "*For the moment. In time, and with careful planning, they will lose both.*"
:   ―Darth Maul and Darth Sidious[[107]](#cite_note-Age_of_Republic_-_Darth_Maul_1-107)

 [![Darth Sidious and Darth Maul were the reigning Sith Lords by the time of the Invasion of Naboo.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2b/Sidious_Maul.png/revision/latest?cb=20201008105820) [![Darth Sidious and Darth Maul were the reigning Sith Lords by the time of the Invasion of Naboo.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2b/Sidious_Maul.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20201008105820)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/2b/Sidious_Maul.png/revision/latest?cb=20201008105820) 

Darth Sidious and Darth Maul were the reigning Sith Lords by the time of the Invasion of Naboo.

 

The Sith remained a distant memory until the last years of the Galactic Republic when Darth Sidious and his apprentice, [Darth Maul](/wiki/Maul "Maul"), revealed themselves to the Jedi.[[2]](#cite_note-Episode_I-2) Although Maul longed to avenge his ancient Sith forebears, he admitted that the Jedi Order was too powerful for the Sith to challenge directly, mainly due to the Jedi's superior numbers and the Galactic Republic's support for the Order. Sidious assured his apprentice that they would undermine the Order's strength with time and careful planning.[[107]](#cite_note-Age_of_Republic_-_Darth_Maul_1-107)

 [![Darth Sidious infiltrated the Galactic Republic's government as Senator Sheev Palpatine of Naboo.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/28/Senator_palpatine.png/revision/latest?cb=20201008105709) [![Darth Sidious infiltrated the Galactic Republic's government as Senator Sheev Palpatine of Naboo.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/28/Senator_palpatine.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20201008105709)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/28/Senator_palpatine.png/revision/latest?cb=20201008105709) 

Darth Sidious infiltrated the Galactic Republic's government as Senator Sheev Palpatine of Naboo.

 

Sidious hid in plain sight as the unassuming [Senator](/wiki/Senator "Senator") Sheev Palpatine of [Naboo](/wiki/Naboo "Naboo"). His double identity allowed him to infiltrate and deceive the [Galactic Senate](/wiki/Galactic_Senate "Galactic Senate"), as well as the inner circle of the [Monarch of Naboo](/wiki/Monarch_of_Naboo "Monarch of Naboo"), [Queen](/wiki/Queen "Queen") [Padmé Amidala](/wiki/Padm%C3%A9_Amidala "Padmé Amidala") whom he served as a close [advisor](/wiki/Advisor "Advisor"). Sidious orchestrated the [Invasion of Naboo](/wiki/Invasion_of_Naboo "Invasion of Naboo") by the [Trade Federation](/wiki/Trade_Federation "Trade Federation") as part of his agenda to accrue more political power at the expense of his [people](/wiki/Naboo_(people) "Naboo (people)") and homeworld. This allowed the Dark Lord to make a play for the galaxy's highest office in his civilian persona and sow the seeds of the Sith's revenge.[[2]](#cite_note-Episode_I-2)

During the [Battle of Naboo](/wiki/Battle_of_Naboo "Battle of Naboo"), Maul killed Jedi Master [Qui-Gon Jinn](/wiki/Qui-Gon_Jinn "Qui-Gon Jinn"), but was defeated and left for dead by Padawan [Obi-Wan Kenobi](/wiki/Obi-Wan_Kenobi "Obi-Wan Kenobi").[[2]](#cite_note-Episode_I-2) Despite the loss of Maul, Sidious discovered a prospective apprentice in [Anakin Skywalker](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker"),[[28]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Sith-28) a child whom the Force was exceptionally strong with. However, Skywalker been discovered and recruited by the Jedi Order.[[2]](#cite_note-Episode_I-2) Nevertheless, Sidious promised to monitor Skywalker's career, intending to turn the Jedi Order's prophesied Chosen One to the dark side of the Force.[[28]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Sith-28) Additionally, Sidious succeeded in his efforts as Palpatine to become [elected](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor_election,_32_BBY "Supreme Chancellor election, 32 BBY") as [Supreme Chancellor](/wiki/Supreme_Chancellor "Supreme Chancellor") of the Galactic Republic.[[2]](#cite_note-Episode_I-2)

#### Separatist Crisis[]

:   "*I told you everything you needed to know on Geonosis all those years ago, Kenobi. You should have joined me. Sifo-Dyas understood, he saw the future. That is why he helped me.*"
:   ―Darth Tyranus, to Obi-Wan Kenobi[[108]](#cite_note-The_Lost_1-108)

 [![Count Dooku was a former Jedi who replaced Maul as Sidious' Sith apprentice, adopting the title of Darth Tyranus.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ac/Sidious_Tyranus.png/revision/latest?cb=20140722221449) [![Count Dooku was a former Jedi who replaced Maul as Sidious' Sith apprentice, adopting the title of Darth Tyranus.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ac/Sidious_Tyranus.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140722221449)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/ac/Sidious_Tyranus.png/revision/latest?cb=20140722221449) 

Count Dooku was a former Jedi who replaced Maul as Sidious' Sith apprentice, adopting the title of Darth Tyranus.

 

Following Maul's apparent demise on Naboo,[[2]](#cite_note-Episode_I-2) Darth Sidious approached the fallen Jedi Master Dooku, who had taken on the title of [Count of Serenno](/wiki/Count_of_Serenno "Count of Serenno"), and offered him the chance to destroy the Jedi Order and reshape the Republic by becoming his new apprentice. Dooku agreed and was given the name Darth Tyranus, desiring both power and the elimination of the corruption that plagued the Republic.[[1]](#cite_note-Episode_II-1) Tyranus also trained the fallen [Dathomirian](/wiki/Dathomirian "Dathomirian") Jedi [Asajj Ventress](/wiki/Asajj_Ventress "Asajj Ventress") as his [assassin](/wiki/Assassin "Assassin") and potential Sith apprentice while still apprenticed to Sidious.[[51]](#cite_note-Nightsisters-51)

 [![The Sith chose a bounty hunter, Jango Fett, as the template for an army of clone troopers.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/18/JangoFettMeetsWithDooku-AORJangoFett1.png/revision/latest?cb=20190111035238) [![The Sith chose a bounty hunter, Jango Fett, as the template for an army of clone troopers.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/18/JangoFettMeetsWithDooku-AORJangoFett1.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20190111035238)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/18/JangoFettMeetsWithDooku-AORJangoFett1.png/revision/latest?cb=20190111035238) 

The Sith chose a bounty hunter, Jango Fett, as the template for an army of clone troopers.

 

For nearly a decade after accepting Sidious's offer, Tyranus helped his new master to implement much of the groundwork necessary to begin the [Clone Wars](/wiki/Clone_Wars "Clone Wars").[[108]](#cite_note-The_Lost_1-108) Jedi Master [Sifo-Dyas](/wiki/Sifo-Dyas "Sifo-Dyas") secretly commissioned the [creation](/wiki/Cloning "Cloning") of an [army](/wiki/Army "Army") of [clone troopers](/wiki/Clone_trooper "Clone trooper"), having foreseen a future conflict through the Force. The Sith took control of Sifo-Dyas' project, however, after arranging his assassination by the [Pyke Syndicate](/wiki/Pyke_Syndicate "Pyke Syndicate").[[109]](#cite_note-Sifo-Dyas_DB-109) Tyranus personally recruited the [bounty hunter](/wiki/Bounty_hunter "Bounty hunter") [Jango Fett](/wiki/Jango_Fett "Jango Fett") to be the [clone template](/wiki/Clone_template "Clone template") of the [Grand Army of the Republic](/wiki/Grand_Army_of_the_Republic "Grand Army of the Republic"),[[110]](#cite_note-AORJF-110) which the Sith intended for the Jedi to lead.[[108]](#cite_note-The_Lost_1-108) An essential part of the Sith's plan was the [behavioral modification biochip](/wiki/Behavioral_modification_biochip "Behavioral modification biochip"); every clone [trooper](/wiki/Trooper "Trooper") was designed with a biochip in their [brain](/wiki/Brain "Brain"), ensuring their compliance with [Order 66](/wiki/Order_66 "Order 66") when the time came to destroy the Jedi.[[111]](#cite_note-Inhibitor_chip_DB-111)

Darth Tyranus, under his public identity as Dooku, reentered the public eye in spectacular fashion, commandeering a Galactic Republic Holonet station in the [Raxus system](/wiki/Raxus_system "Raxus system") and delivering a rousing speech in which he thoroughly lambasted the corruption and shortcomings of the Republic. He then began to rally rebellious star systems to his cause and secretly allied himself with powerful commercial entities, resulting in the formation of the [Confederacy of Independent Systems](/wiki/Confederacy_of_Independent_Systems "Confederacy of Independent Systems").[[18]](#cite_note-Tarkin-18)

 [![The Separatist leadership was controlled by Tyranus, who in turn, answered to Sidious.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bb/JourneysBeginnings-SepCouncil.png/revision/latest?cb=20241019033343) [![The Separatist leadership was controlled by Tyranus, who in turn, answered to Sidious.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bb/JourneysBeginnings-SepCouncil.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20241019033343)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/bb/JourneysBeginnings-SepCouncil.png/revision/latest?cb=20241019033343) 

The Separatist leadership was controlled by Tyranus, who in turn, answered to Sidious.

 

War broke out as both the Confederacy's [droid armies](/wiki/Separatist_Droid_Army "Separatist Droid Army") and the newly-formed Grand Army of the Republic fought over the desert-landscape of [Geonosis](/wiki/Geonosis "Geonosis") after the extent of Tyranus' secret alliance with the [Trade Federation](/wiki/Trade_Federation "Trade Federation"), the [Techno Union](/wiki/Techno_Union "Techno Union"), the [InterGalactic Banking Clan](/wiki/InterGalactic_Banking_Clan "InterGalactic Banking Clan"), the [Corporate Alliance](/wiki/Corporate_Alliance "Corporate Alliance"), and the [Commerce Guild](/wiki/Commerce_Guild "Commerce Guild") was revealed. Though the Republic was able to score a victory, Tyranus and the rest of the [Separatist leadership](/wiki/Executive_Separatist_Council "Executive Separatist Council") were able to escape the planet.[[1]](#cite_note-Episode_II-1)

In preparation for the upcoming galactic-scale conflict and its aftermath, Tyranus traveled to Coruscant's industrial district, known as [the Works](/wiki/The_Works "The Works"), after the [First Battle of Geonosis](/wiki/First_Battle_of_Geonosis "First Battle of Geonosis"), where he met with Sidious and delivered the "good news" of the war's beginning, as well as presented him with the plans for the [DS-1 Death Star Mobile Battle Station](/wiki/DS-1_Orbital_Battle_Station "DS-1 Orbital Battle Station").[[1]](#cite_note-Episode_II-1)

#### Clone Wars[]

:   "*I have good news for you, my Lord. The war has begun.*"  
    "*Excellent. Everything is going as planned.*"
:   ―Darth Tyranus and Darth Sidious — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/99/TheWarHasBegun-AOTC.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250403184749)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:TheWarHasBegun-AOTC.flac "File:TheWarHasBegun-AOTC.flac"))[[1]](#cite_note-Episode_II-1)

 [![During the Clone Wars, the Sith controlled the Galactic Republic and the Confederacy of Independent Systems.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/20/Sith_lair_The_Works.png/revision/latest?cb=20180211184711) [![During the Clone Wars, the Sith controlled the Galactic Republic and the Confederacy of Independent Systems.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/20/Sith_lair_The_Works.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180211184711)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/2/20/Sith_lair_The_Works.png/revision/latest?cb=20180211184711) 

During the Clone Wars, the Sith controlled the Galactic Republic and the Confederacy of Independent Systems.

 

In the aftermath of the battle at [Geonosis](/wiki/Geonosis "Geonosis"), the Jedi transitioned from peacekeepers to [generals](/wiki/Jedi_General "Jedi General") and [commanders](/wiki/Jedi_Commander "Jedi Commander"), ranks that they were formerly denied due to the Jedi Code.[[1]](#cite_note-Episode_II-1) During the war, Dooku was briefly captured by the [Ohnaka Gang](/wiki/Ohnaka_Gang "Ohnaka Gang").[[112]](#cite_note-Dooku_Captured-112) With most civilians in the galaxy unaware of what a "Sith" was,[[113]](#cite_note-Revival-113) pirate leader [Hondo Ohnaka](/wiki/Hondo_Ohnaka "Hondo Ohnaka") indeed believed Dooku was simply a rogue Jedi who had broken away from the Republic. Upon hearing Dooku declare himself to be a Sith Lord, Ohnaka remained unconcerned and focused on the great bounty he would gain by ransoming the Separatist leader to the Republic.[[112]](#cite_note-Dooku_Captured-112) However, Dooku ultimately escaped when Ohnaka was distracted by Kenobi and Skywalker, who were also captured to be ransomed.[[114]](#cite_note-The_Gungan_General-114) Dooku decided against telling his master the details of the incident, believing it to be an embarrassment.[[115]](#cite_note-Dooku_Captured_Story-115)

 [![Savage Opress, the brother of Darth Maul, was briefly trained as the secret apprentice of Darth Tyranus.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d1/SavageScissored-WOTM.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110924042356) [![Savage Opress, the brother of Darth Maul, was briefly trained as the secret apprentice of Darth Tyranus.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d1/SavageScissored-WOTM.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20110924042356)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d1/SavageScissored-WOTM.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20110924042356) 

Savage Opress, the brother of Darth Maul, was briefly trained as the secret apprentice of Darth Tyranus.

 

On her tasks for the Sith, Ventress engaged Anakin Skywalker, Obi-Wan Kenobi, and [Ahsoka Tano](/wiki/Ahsoka_Tano "Ahsoka Tano") in [lightsaber duels](/wiki/Lightsaber_duel "Lightsaber duel") on numerous occasions.[[116]](#cite_note-Hidden_Enemy-116)[[117]](#cite_note-Cloak_of_Darkness-117) While loyal, she was ultimately betrayed by her Master on the orders of Darth Sidious. Dooku soon after traveled to Dathomir to meet with the Nightsisters in hopes of finding a new apprentice.[[51]](#cite_note-Nightsisters-51) Dooku and the Nightsisters eventually decided on a young [Zabrak](/wiki/Zabrak "Zabrak") named [Savage Opress](/wiki/Savage_Opress "Savage Opress"), brother of the long-presumed dead Darth Maul. However, Asajj Ventress sought revenge for Dooku's treachery and used Opress as a means of attaining her goal.[[58]](#cite_note-Monster-58) Torn between two demanding masters, Opress eventually turned on both Dooku and Ventress.[[118]](#cite_note-Witches_of_the_Mist-118)

Returning to the Nightsisters, Opress found that his brother, Maul, had not been killed as previously believed.[[118]](#cite_note-Witches_of_the_Mist-118) Maul had survived his injuries on Naboo because of his sheer reliance on the dark side and was living in the junk heaps of [Lotho Minor](/wiki/Lotho_Minor "Lotho Minor").
