However, Maul's tragic events had driven him to insanity. He remembered only one word: "Kenobi." Guided by an [Anacondan](/wiki/Anacondan "Anacondan") named [Morley](/wiki/Morley "Morley"),[[119]](#cite_note-Brothers-119) Opress was able to return Maul to the Nightsisters for treatment. Now fully healed by the Nightsisters' magic and given a pair of new robotic legs, Maul began a hunt for the man who had nearly destroyed his life, Obi-Wan Kenobi.[[120]](#cite_note-Revenge-120)

 [![Sidious killed Opress and captured Maul, ending their claim to the Sith mantle and enforcing the Rule of Two.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a0/SidiousVsNightbrothers-TL.png/revision/latest?cb=20131025201653) [![Sidious killed Opress and captured Maul, ending their claim to the Sith mantle and enforcing the Rule of Two.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a0/SidiousVsNightbrothers-TL.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20131025201653)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a0/SidiousVsNightbrothers-TL.png/revision/latest?cb=20131025201653) 

Sidious killed Opress and captured Maul, ending their claim to the Sith mantle and enforcing the Rule of Two.

 

His revenge scheme eventually ended with Maul's [control](/wiki/Takeover_of_Mandalore "Takeover of Mandalore") of [Mandalore](/wiki/Mandalore "Mandalore")[[121]](#cite_note-Shades_of_Reason-121) and the death of [Satine Kryze](/wiki/Satine_Kryze "Satine Kryze"). However, Darth Sidious sensed his former apprentice's action and his stance as a potential rival, and [traveled](/wiki/Mandalorian_Civil_War_(19_BBY) "Mandalorian Civil War (19 BBY)") to Mandalore to put an end to it. He killed Opress and took Maul captive,[[122]](#cite_note-The_Lawless-122) locking him away in an old mountaintop prison known as [the Spire](/wiki/Spire_(Stygeon_Prime) "Spire (Stygeon Prime)"), in an elaborate Sith gambit to settle a longstanding and deadly dispute with the Nightsisters.[[123]](#cite_note-SonOfDathomir1-123)

Later during the war, [Yoda](/wiki/Yoda "Yoda") [visited](/wiki/Mission_to_Moraband "Mission to Moraband") Moraband, the Sith homeworld. The Jedi Master encountered an illusory spectre of the ancient Sith Darth Bane, who was buried on the barren planet and battled Sidious on a spiritual plane as the result of an ancient, arcane Sith [ritual](/wiki/Dark_illusion "Dark illusion"). Through his experience, Yoda gained a new enlightenment about the Force that the Sith did not foresee.[[17]](#cite_note-Sacrifice-17)

#### Revenge of the Sith[]

##### Seduction of the Chosen One[]

:   "*Good is a point of view, Anakin. The Sith and the Jedi are similar in almost every way, including their quest for greater power.*"  
    "*The Sith rely on their passion for their strength. They think inwards, only about themselves.*"  
    "*And the Jedi don't?*"  
    "*The Jedi are selfless. They only care about others.*"
:   ―Darth Sidious and Anakin Skywalker[[24]](#cite_note-Episode_III-24)

 [![After Tyranus' death, the Jedi Knight Anakin Skywalker became Sidious' new apprentice as Darth Vader.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/42/SithTeachings-Convergence.png/revision/latest?cb=20201129074930) [![After Tyranus' death, the Jedi Knight Anakin Skywalker became Sidious' new apprentice as Darth Vader.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/42/SithTeachings-Convergence.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20201129074930)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/42/SithTeachings-Convergence.png/revision/latest?cb=20201129074930) 

After Tyranus' death, the Jedi Knight Anakin Skywalker became Sidious' new apprentice as Darth Vader.

 

After three years of the Clone Wars, Darth Sidious' grand scheme was almost complete. He [sacrificed](/wiki/Battle_of_Coruscant "Battle of Coruscant") and betrayed Count Dooku to a violent killing by Anakin Skywalker, to manipulate the young Jedi. As Palpatine, he told Anakin a Sith [legend](/wiki/Tragedy_of_Darth_Plagueis_the_Wise "Tragedy of Darth Plagueis the Wise") about Darth Plagueis the Wise. Plagueis, through the dark side, had gained the ability to keep people from dying until his apprentice killed him in his sleep. This story entranced Anakin, who was desperate to learn this power to save his wife, Padmé Amidala.[[24]](#cite_note-Episode_III-24)

Eventually, Palpatine revealed himself as Sidious and converted Anakin to the dark side. Jedi Master [Mace Windu](/wiki/Mace_Windu "Mace Windu") tried to [arrest](/wiki/Duel_in_Palpatine%27s_office "Duel in Palpatine's office") the Dark Lord but was killed after Anakin betrayed Mace and the Jedi. After this, Anakin pledged himself to service under his new Sith Master, Sidious, and became Darth Vader.[[24]](#cite_note-Episode_III-24)

##### The New Order[]

:   "*Once more the Sith will rule the galaxy, and we shall have peace.*"
:   ―Darth Sidious[[24]](#cite_note-Episode_III-24)

 [![With the fall of the Jedi, the Sith returned to power through Sidious' ascension as Emperor of the Galactic Empire.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/ff/Declaration.png/revision/latest?cb=20240221001415) [![With the fall of the Jedi, the Sith returned to power through Sidious' ascension as Emperor of the Galactic Empire.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/ff/Declaration.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20240221001415)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/f/ff/Declaration.png/revision/latest?cb=20240221001415) 

With the fall of the Jedi, the Sith returned to power through Sidious' ascension as Emperor of the Galactic Empire.

 

With Windu's attack and a new Sith apprentice at his side, Sidious realized this was the perfect opportunity for him to destroy the Jedi. He ordered Vader to lead the [501st Legion](/wiki/501st_Legion "501st Legion")'s [attack on the Jedi Temple](/wiki/Operation:_Knightfall "Operation: Knightfall"), and then go to the [Mustafar system](/wiki/Mustafar_system "Mustafar system") to [wipe](/wiki/Mission_to_Mustafar "Mission to Mustafar") out the [Separatist Council](/wiki/Executive_Separatist_Council "Executive Separatist Council"). With Vader at the temple, Sidious unleashed order 66, which led to the Clones' biochips activating and brainwashing them into murdering the Jedi.[[111]](#cite_note-Inhibitor_chip_DB-111) Thousands of Jedi across the galaxy were then betrayed and killed by their clone troopers. Prior to Vader arriving on Mustafar to execute the Separatist Council, Sidious tricked the council into believing that Vader would protect them. After Vader slaughtered the Separatists, Vader followed Sidious's third order by shutting down the droid army, which ended the Clone Wars. In the political arena, he reorganized the Republic using the powers given to him as a result of the Clone Wars to transform the Galactic Republic into the Galactic Empire to restore the Sith Empire, installing himself as [Emperor](/wiki/Galactic_Emperor "Galactic Emperor"). Once more, the Sith ruled the galaxy, unbeknownst to all but the few surviving Jedi.[[24]](#cite_note-Episode_III-24)

### Rise of the Galactic Empire[]

#### Reign of the Sith[]

:   "*And my apprentices? Darth Maul was a loss, but Darth Tyranus…he was a proton torpedo. He served his purpose and was gone. I had a…*superior *candidate in mind. We did it, Vader. The Jedi destroyed! The Republic a shattered corpse for me to resurrect as a puppet! And you, Vader—the boy transformed into the man you were destined to be…*"
:   ―Darth Sidious, to Darth Vader[[79]](#cite_note-Darth_Vader_20-79)

 [![The Sith ruled the galaxy for a generation, consolidating the Empire and hunting the few Jedi who survived Order 66.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6e/Vader_Sidious.png/revision/latest?cb=20130205215534) [![The Sith ruled the galaxy for a generation, consolidating the Empire and hunting the few Jedi who survived Order 66.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6e/Vader_Sidious.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20130205215534)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/6/6e/Vader_Sidious.png/revision/latest?cb=20130205215534) 

The Sith ruled the galaxy for a generation, consolidating the Empire and hunting the few Jedi who survived Order 66.

 

Following the reorganization of the Republic and [purging](/wiki/Great_Jedi_Purge "Great Jedi Purge") of the Jedi Order, Darth Sidious and Vader ruled over the First Galactic Empire for over twenty years until the [Battle of Endor](/wiki/Battle_of_Endor "Battle of Endor"). The two Sith Lords established a cadre of Dark Side wielders known as the [Inquisitorius](/wiki/Inquisitorius "Inquisitorius").[[124]](#cite_note-Epic_Battles-124) The Inquisitors were tasked with hunting down Jedi Purge survivors and preventing [Force-sensitive](/wiki/Force-sensitive "Force-sensitive") [children](/wiki/Youngling "Youngling") from becoming Jedi. The leading Inquisitor was a [Pau'an](/wiki/Pau%27an "Pau'an") [Grand Inquisitor](/wiki/The_Grand_Inquisitor "The Grand Inquisitor"),[[125]](#cite_note-Spark_of_Rebellion-125) who was a former [Jedi Sentinel](/wiki/Jedi_Sentinel "Jedi Sentinel") and Knight.[[126]](#cite_note-Shroud_of_Darkness-126) The Inquisitors were trained by Vader and wielded double-bladed spinning [lightsabers](/wiki/Lightsaber "Lightsaber").[[124]](#cite_note-Epic_Battles-124)

#### Momin's return[]

Sometime into the [Imperial Era](/wiki/Imperial_Era "Imperial Era"), Vader embarked on a mission to [Mustafar](/wiki/Mustafar "Mustafar"). With him, he took the [Chief Imperial Architect](/wiki/Chief_Imperial_Architect "Chief Imperial Architect") [Colonel](/wiki/Colonel "Colonel") [Alva Brenne](/wiki/Alva_Brenne "Alva Brenne"), her assistant [Lieutenant](/wiki/Lieutenant "Lieutenant") [Roggo](/wiki/Roggo "Roggo"), and the mask that once belonged to Momin. Sidious had assured Vader that Momin's mask would guide him during his studies there. Whilst on the planet, Vader meditated in the [Sith cave](/wiki/Sith_cave "Sith cave") there. That was when Momin's mask possessed Roggo and Momin used his body to design a structure. When Brenne discovered this, she was shot dead, alerting Vader to the situation. Vader killed Roggo[[36]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_21-36) and removed the mask from his body.[[14]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith_22-14)

 [![Fortress Vader was a Sith stronghold constructed on Mustafar during the rise of the Empire.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/ce/MominPresentsFortressVader-2017DarthVader23.png/revision/latest?cb=20181129061321) [![Fortress Vader was a Sith stronghold constructed on Mustafar during the rise of the Empire.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/ce/MominPresentsFortressVader-2017DarthVader23.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20181129061321)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/c/ce/MominPresentsFortressVader-2017DarthVader23.png/revision/latest?cb=20181129061321) 

Fortress Vader was a Sith stronghold constructed on Mustafar during the rise of the Empire.

 

Vader took it to the cave and reached into it using the Force. Momin revealed himself to Vader and told him his story, before attempting to possess him too. Vader resisted but came to let the mask take control of a [Mustafarian](/wiki/Mustafarian "Mustafarian"), giving Momin a body again. The two discussed the structure Momin had designed and Momin claimed it could tune the energies of the dark side locus on Mustafar, opening the door to the dark side that could resurrect Padmé Amidala. Vader subsequently agreed to let Momin build [Fortress Vader](/wiki/Fortress_Vader "Fortress Vader").[[14]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith_22-14)

In truth, Momin hoped to use the energies to resurrect his own body. As the [Battle of Fortress Vader](/wiki/Battle_of_Fortress_Vader "Battle of Fortress Vader") raged outside, Momin successfully revived himself.[[127]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_23-127) In his duel with Vader, Momin insulted the current state of the Sith as "Jedi-obsessed weaklings," remarking that it saddened him and further claiming it disgusted the dark side itself. Vader, in the end, triumphed over the ancient Sith and killed Momin once more. All the same, his mask survived again[[128]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_24-128) and was returned to Sidious by Vader, who tried and failed to use the portal to resurrect Amidala. For its failure, he destroyed the gateway.[[129]](#cite_note-Encyclopedia_Maul-129) Nevertheless, the incident had concluded with Vader fully committing himself on the path of the dark side.[[130]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_25-130)

#### Spark of Rebellion[]

 [![The insurgents on Ryloth failed in their efforts to assassinate the Emperor and his apprentice.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b0/Mission_to_Ryloth.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170318083212) [![The insurgents on Ryloth failed in their efforts to assassinate the Emperor and his apprentice.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b0/Mission_to_Ryloth.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20170318083212)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/b/b0/Mission_to_Ryloth.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20170318083212) 

The insurgents on Ryloth failed in their efforts to assassinate the Emperor and his apprentice.

 

Five years after the end of the Clone Wars, the [Free Ryloth Movement](/wiki/Free_Ryloth_Movement "Free Ryloth Movement") led by [Cham Syndulla](/wiki/Cham_Syndulla "Cham Syndulla") embarked on a [large-scale operation](/wiki/Mission_to_Ryloth "Mission to Ryloth") to assassinate the Emperor and Vader. Cham wanted to kill the two Sith Lords to bring about the demise of the Empire. However, Sidious had anticipated Cham's move, and the two Sith eluded Cham's attempts to assassinate them. This operation dealt a major blow to the Free Ryloth rebels, who were forced deeper underground, and also led to the exposure of Colonel [Belkor Dray](/wiki/Belkor_Dray "Belkor Dray") as a [traitor](/wiki/Treason "Treason"). Despite Sidious' hopes, he failed to stamp out the sparks of the growing rebellion.[[23]](#cite_note-LOTS-23)

Among those opposed to Palpatine's rule was [Luthen Rael](/wiki/Luthen_Rael "Luthen Rael"), who maintained the cover of an innocent artifact collector and dealer while secretly building up a [rebel network](/wiki/Axis_network "Axis network").[[131]](#cite_note-Announcement-131) Among the artifacts in Rael's collection were a Sith holocron he kept in the back of his [Galactic Antiquities and Objects of Interest](/wiki/Galactic_Antiquities_and_Objects_of_Interest "Galactic Antiquities and Objects of Interest") store[[132]](#cite_note-Luthen_Gallery-132) and several pieces of [Sith armor](/wiki/Sith_armor "Sith armor").[[131]](#cite_note-Announcement-131) After the outbreak of the Lothal insurgency about four years before the [Battle of Yavin](/wiki/Battle_of_Yavin "Battle of Yavin"), Sidious dispatched Vader to hunt down the [Spectres](/wiki/Spectres "Spectres"), who were part of the growing rebellion. Vader lured the Spectres into a [trap](/wiki/Mission_to_Lothal_(4_BBY) "Mission to Lothal (4 BBY)") on [Lothal](/wiki/Lothal "Lothal") in an attempt to track down the [Phoenix Cell](/wiki/Phoenix_Cell "Phoenix Cell"). Vader led an [attack](/wiki/Attack_on_Phoenix_Squadron_(4_BBY) "Attack on Phoenix Squadron (4 BBY)") on the Phoenix fleet which destroyed the rebel flagship *[Phoenix Home](/wiki/Phoenix_Home "Phoenix Home")* but failed to destroy the rebellion. During the skirmish, Vader discovered that his former apprentice Ahsoka Tano was still alive. Under Sidious' orders, he dispatched more Inquisitors to hunt down the Jedi Purge survivor [Kanan Jarrus](/wiki/Kanan_Jarrus "Kanan Jarrus") and his apprentice [Ezra Bridger](/wiki/Ezra_Bridger "Ezra Bridger").[[133]](#cite_note-Siege_of_Lothal-133)

#### Struggle on Malachor[]

:   "*The power within will soon serve the Emperor.*"
:   ―Darth Vader[[20]](#cite_note-Twilight-20)

 [![Darth Vader was sent to an ancient Sith temple on Malachor, where he intended to secure its power for his Sith Master.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4e/Darth_Vader_Decending_TotA.png/revision/latest?cb=20180831023437) [![Darth Vader was sent to an ancient Sith temple on Malachor, where he intended to secure its power for his Sith Master.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4e/Darth_Vader_Decending_TotA.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180831023437)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/4/4e/Darth_Vader_Decending_TotA.png/revision/latest?cb=20180831023437) 

Darth Vader was sent to an ancient Sith temple on Malachor, where he intended to secure its power for his Sith Master.

 

A year later, Vader visited the [Lothal Jedi Temple](/wiki/Lothal_Jedi_Temple "Lothal Jedi Temple") where the [Fifth Brother](/wiki/Fifth_Brother "Fifth Brother") and the [Seventh Sister](/wiki/Seventh_Sister "Seventh Sister") had attempted to capture Bridger, Jarrus, and Tano. Vader remarked that the Emperor would be pleased with their discovery. When the Fifth Brother remarked that the power of the Jedi was growing, Vader responded that it would be their undoing.[[126]](#cite_note-Shroud_of_Darkness-126) The Sith Lords later took an interest in the Sith temple on Malachor, which was reputed to be home to a weapon capable of destroying all life. Vader sent another Inquisitor called the [Eighth Brother](/wiki/Eighth_Brother "Eighth Brother") to hunt down a "shadow" and to obtain a [Sith holocron](/wiki/Sith_holocron_(Malachor) "Sith holocron (Malachor)").[[20]](#cite_note-Twilight-20)

Bridger, Jarrus, and Tano encountered the former Sith apprentice Maul—who was the "shadow" that Vader sent the Eighth Brother to hunt—in the Malachor Sith Temple. Maul had become stranded on Malachor several years prior and had discovered a secret inside the Sith temple that would allow them to destroy the Sith. However, he lacked the strength to do so on his own. Maul managed to befriend Ezra and the two Force-wielders succeeded in obtaining the Sith holocron. Maul later helped the Jedi drive several Inquisitors away. Despite Jarrus and Tano's distrust, Maul managed to convince them to help him by teasing the opportunity of destroying the Sith once and for all.[[20]](#cite_note-Twilight-20)

 [![Ahsoka Tano confronted Darth Vader in the Malachor temple, and discovered his former identity as her Jedi mentor, Anakin Skywalker.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3d/Forestall-CM.png/revision/latest?cb=20201217021723) [![Ahsoka Tano confronted Darth Vader in the Malachor temple, and discovered his former identity as her Jedi mentor, Anakin Skywalker.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3d/Forestall-CM.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20201217021723)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3d/Forestall-CM.png/revision/latest?cb=20201217021723) 

Ahsoka Tano confronted Darth Vader in the Malachor temple, and discovered his former identity as her Jedi mentor, Anakin Skywalker.

 

Maul convinced Ezra to place the Sith holocron in the obelisk at the top of the temple complex. He then helped Jarrus and Tano kill the Inquisitors before turning on both of them. Eventually, Maul blinded Jarrus. Despite this, the Jedi Knight defeated Maul in combat and pushed him off the edge of the temple. Meanwhile, Ezra discovered that the Sith holocron was the key to reactivating the Sith temple, which was a powerful superweapon capable of destroying life. Shortly later, Darth Vader arrived to claim the temple's power for the Sith. Darth Vader fought with Ahsoka while Jarrus and Bridger removed the holocron; triggering the temple's implosion. Bridger and Jarrus escaped the temple, but Vader and Tano were trapped inside when the Temple began to implode. Vader and Tano survived and parted company.[[20]](#cite_note-Twilight-20)

Later, Bridger came under the influence of the Sith Holocron, which was inhabited by an entity called [Presence](/wiki/Presence "Presence"). Under the holocron's guidance, Ezra learned more aggressive combat techniques including forcing an [AT-DP walker](/wiki/All_Terrain_Defense_Pod "All Terrain Defense Pod") [driver](/wiki/Imperial_combat_driver "Imperial combat driver") to attack his comrades and walk his machine off a bridge. Bridger's use of the Sith Holocron strained relations with his master Jarrus, who confiscated it. Jarrus later met a powerful Force-wielder called the [Bendu](/wiki/Bendu "Bendu"), who formed a middle ground between the light and dark sides. He advised Jarrus that an object could be used for both good and evil and that only the person had the power to change it. Jarrus left the Sith holocron in the Bendu's care.[[134]](#cite_note-Steps_into_Shadow-134)

 [![The former Sith Lord Maul enlisted the unwitting aid of Padawan Ezra Bridger in his quest to find Jedi Master Obi-Wan Kenobi.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e7/The_Holocrons_of_Fate_Episode_Guide.png/revision/latest?cb=20161001154010) [![The former Sith Lord Maul enlisted the unwitting aid of Padawan Ezra Bridger in his quest to find Jedi Master Obi-Wan Kenobi.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e7/The_Holocrons_of_Fate_Episode_Guide.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161001154010)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e7/The_Holocrons_of_Fate_Episode_Guide.png/revision/latest?cb=20161001154010) 

The former Sith Lord Maul enlisted the unwitting aid of Padawan Ezra Bridger in his quest to find Jedi Master Obi-Wan Kenobi.

 

Maul, who was revealed to have survived the events on Malachor, later [captured](/wiki/Maul%27s_capture_of_the_Ghost_crew "Maul's capture of the Ghost crew") Jarrus and Bridger's rebel friends and used them as hostages to force the two Jedi to bring him the Sith holocron and [Kanan's Jedi holocron](/wiki/Kanan_Jarrus%27_holocron "Kanan Jarrus' holocron"). Jarrus and Bridger recovered the Sith holocron from the Bendu, who warned them that Maul planned to combine the power of the holocrons to provide clarity of vision. After rendezvousing with Maul, Bridger and the former Sith combined the two holocrons. Bridger wanted to find a way to destroy the Sith while Maul was looking for hope. The holocrons projected a vision of [twin](/wiki/Tatoo_I "Tatoo I") [suns](/wiki/Tatoo_II "Tatoo II"), an old enemy of Maul, and offered to show Bridger the "key" to destroying the Sith. However, Jarrus convinced his apprentice to look away, and the two holocrons separated. Maul took the opportunity to escape into space.[[135]](#cite_note-Holocrons_of_Fate-135)

 [![Bridger refused to become Maul's apprentice and attempted to find Kenobi, believing he held the key to the Sith's destruction.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d6/Maul_and_Ezra_Nightsister_lair.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161212104030) [![Bridger refused to become Maul's apprentice and attempted to find Kenobi, believing he held the key to the Sith's destruction.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d6/Maul_and_Ezra_Nightsister_lair.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20161212104030)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d6/Maul_and_Ezra_Nightsister_lair.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20161212104030) 

Bridger refused to become Maul's apprentice and attempted to find Kenobi, believing he held the key to the Sith's destruction.

 

Using the fragments of Bridger's memories in his mind, Maul tracked the rebels down to their [base](/wiki/Chopper_Base "Chopper Base") on [Atollon](/wiki/Atollon "Atollon"). Using the dark side of the Force, Maul manifested in Bridger's visions. Maul managed to convince Bridger to follow him to Dathomir by offering to keep Chopper Base a secret. At the [Nightsister lair](/wiki/Nightsister_lair "Nightsister lair"), Maul and Bridger underwent a ritual to uncover the remaining fragments of the holocrons in each others' minds. After drinking a magic potion, Maul learned that Master Kenobi was still living on the [planet](/wiki/Tatooine "Tatooine") with twin suns while Bridger learned that Kenobi held the key to destroying the Sith. The two were then attacked by the spirits of the Nightsisters, who demanded payment in flesh and blood for their services. Jarrus and the [Mandalorian](/wiki/Mandalorian "Mandalorian") weapons expert [Sabine Wren](/wiki/Sabine_Wren "Sabine Wren") arrived to confront Maul but were possessed by the spirits. Bridger and Maul managed to flee outside the lair. When Maul offered Bridger a place as his apprentice, the young Jedi refused to abandon his friends. After exorcising Jarrus and Wren, the three resolved to find the planet with twin suns and to reach Kenobi before Maul could kill him.[[136]](#cite_note-Visions_and_Voices-136)

### Galactic Civil War[]

:   "*We kept the skeleton of the Republic for nearly twenty years while the Death Star was constructed. Twenty years, my apprentice. All that planning is now a layer of dust orbiting around Yavin. Now, we no longer have the Senate to hold order. We do not have the Death Star to force it. Our greatest weapon is gone. Our production is in ashes. We are besieged. In all these years, we have never skirted closer to disaster.*"
:   ―Darth Sidious, to Darth Vader[[137]](#cite_note-Darth_Vader_(2015)_1-137)

 [![The Death Star was a superweapon loosely based on an ancient Sith design.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a1/DeathStarLaserConstruction.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160410023743) [![The Death Star was a superweapon loosely based on an ancient Sith design.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a1/DeathStarLaserConstruction.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160410023743)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a1/DeathStarLaserConstruction.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160410023743) 

The Death Star was a superweapon loosely based on an ancient Sith design.

 

In the years leading up to the Battle of Yavin, the Empire faced a growing rebellion that had grown into the [Alliance to Restore the Republic](/wiki/Alliance_to_Restore_the_Republic "Alliance to Restore the Republic"). In secret, the Emperor commissioned the building of the [Death Star](/wiki/DS-1_Orbital_Battle_Station "DS-1 Orbital Battle Station"), a massive superweapon capable of destroying entire worlds. After rebel elements [stole](/wiki/Battle_of_Scarif "Battle of Scarif") the [Death Star plans](/wiki/Death_Star_plans "Death Star plans"), Vader led a [secret mission to Tatooine](/wiki/Secret_mission_to_Tatooine "Secret mission to Tatooine") which ended with the capture of [Princess](/wiki/Princess "Princess") [Leia Organa](/wiki/Leia_Skywalker_Organa_Solo "Leia Skywalker Organa Solo"), the adopted daughter of [Bail Organa](/wiki/Bail_Prestor_Organa "Bail Prestor Organa") and one of the offspring of Anakin Skywalker. Shortly thereafter, the Emperor dissolved the [Imperial Senate](/wiki/Imperial_Senate "Imperial Senate") and ordered [Alderaan](/wiki/Alderaan "Alderaan")'s [destruction](/wiki/Destruction_of_Alderaan "Destruction of Alderaan").[[25]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-25)

Lord Vader and [Grand Moff](/wiki/Grand_Moff "Grand Moff") [Wilhuff Tarkin](/wiki/Wilhuff_Tarkin "Wilhuff Tarkin") presided over Alderaan's destruction in the presence of Princess Leia. Before they could terminate Leia, she was rescued by a group of travelers including Anakin's son [Luke Skywalker](/wiki/Luke_Skywalker "Luke Skywalker"), the smugglers [Han Solo](/wiki/Han_Solo "Han Solo") and [Chewbacca](/wiki/Chewbacca "Chewbacca"), the droids [C-3PO](/wiki/C-3PO "C-3PO") and [R2-D2](/wiki/R2-D2 "R2-D2"), and the Jedi Master Kenobi. While the other rebels escaped aboard the *[Millennium Falcon](/wiki/Millennium_Falcon "Millennium Falcon")*, Kenobi sacrificed his life to delay Vader. Leia and her rescuers retreated to the rebel base on Yavin 4. The Death Star traveled to Yavin base in a bid to destroy the Rebel Alliance once and for all but this plan was ruined by a rebel [starfighter](/wiki/Starfighter "Starfighter") force. During the Battle of Yavin, Vader sensed that the Force was strong in the rebel pilot Skywalker; who fired the missile that destroyed the Death Star, Vader, however, survived the destruction.[[25]](#cite_note-Episode_IV-25)

 [![The Sith sought to prevent Luke Skywalker from becoming a Jedi by turning him to the dark side of the Force.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/33/DarthVader2020-5-Sprouse-textless.png/revision/latest?cb=20210523171450) [![The Sith sought to prevent Luke Skywalker from becoming a Jedi by turning him to the dark side of the Force.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/33/DarthVader2020-5-Sprouse-textless.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20210523171450)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/33/DarthVader2020-5-Sprouse-textless.png/revision/latest?cb=20210523171450) 

The Sith sought to prevent Luke Skywalker from becoming a Jedi by turning him to the dark side of the Force.

 

Three years after the events on Yavin and following the [Battle of Hoth](/wiki/Battle_of_Hoth "Battle of Hoth"), the Emperor disclosed that Luke was one of the offspring of Anakin Skywalker, though this was something Vader already knew. Vader believed that Luke would be a powerful ally if he could be turned. The Emperor charged Vader with winning Luke over and destroying him if he refused to turn to the dark side. During that time Luke had traveled to [Dagobah](/wiki/Dagobah "Dagobah"), where he had been trained by Yoda, a Jedi Master who was once the leader of the Jedi Order. Vader managed to capture Leia, Han, C-3PO and Chewbacca in [Cloud City](/wiki/Cloud_City "Cloud City") on [Bespin](/wiki/Bespin "Bespin"). Sensing the danger that his friends were in, Luke left his training and traveled to Cloud City where Vader was waiting for him. During their [confrontation](/wiki/Duel_on_Cloud_City "Duel on Cloud City"), Vader severed Luke's right hand and revealed that he was Luke's father. Despite the pain, Luke refused to join Vader, threw himself down a [vane](/wiki/Weather_scanner_vane "Weather scanner vane") and escaped.[[138]](#cite_note-Episode_V-138)

### Fall of the Sith[]

:   "*Now, fulfill your destiny and take your father's place at my side.*"  
    "*Never. I'll never turn to the dark side. You failed, Your Highness. I'm a Jedi, like my father before me.*"  
    "*So be it, Jedi.*"
:   ―Darth Sidious and Luke Skywalker[[43]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-43)

 [![Construction of the second Death Star was overseen by both Sith Lords in the days leading up to the Battle of Endor.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0d/GreejatusAndFriends-ROTJ.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120113180412) [![Construction of the second Death Star was overseen by both Sith Lords in the days leading up to the Battle of Endor.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0d/GreejatusAndFriends-ROTJ.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20120113180412)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/0d/GreejatusAndFriends-ROTJ.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120113180412) 

Construction of the second Death Star was overseen by both Sith Lords in the days leading up to the Battle of Endor.

 

In secret, the Emperor directed the building of a [second Death Star](/wiki/DS-2_Death_Star_II_Mobile_Battle_Station "DS-2 Death Star II Mobile Battle Station") above the forest moon of [Endor](/wiki/Endor "Endor"). In an attempt to destroy the rebellion once and for all, the Emperor arranged for intelligence on the second Death Star to be leaked to [Bothan](/wiki/Bothan "Bothan") spies. Using this information, the Rebel Alliance made preparations to launch an attack on the second Death Star. Before the Battle of Endor, Vader traveled to the second Death Star to warn [Moff](/wiki/Moff "Moff") [Tiaan Jerjerrod](/wiki/Tiaan_Jerjerrod "Tiaan Jerjerrod") to accelerate construction. Shortly later, Sidious traveled to the battle station to oversee the final construction stages.[[43]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-43)

Luke confronted Yoda and the [Force spirit](/wiki/Force_spirit "Force spirit") of Kenobi about Vader's claims on Bespin, and accepted that the Sith Lord was in fact his father, Anakin Skywalker, after his mentors confirmed it. Luke accompanied the Rebels to Endor with the intention to confront Vader, believing that he could help the former Jedi return to the light side. Likewise, the Emperor sought to turn Luke to the dark side in order to replace Vader as an apprentice. On the second Death Star, Luke confronted Sidious who wanted to provoke Luke's anger by having the Imperial Navy engage the Rebel fleet, thus putting his friends' lives at risk.[[43]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-43)

 [![The prophecy of the Chosen One came to pass when Sidious and Vader died as the last Sith Lords.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/dd/Vader_Grabs_Palpatine.png/revision/latest?cb=20140715024315) [![The prophecy of the Chosen One came to pass when Sidious and Vader died as the last Sith Lords.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/dd/Vader_Grabs_Palpatine.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20140715024315)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/dd/Vader_Grabs_Palpatine.png/revision/latest?cb=20140715024315) 

The prophecy of the Chosen One came to pass when Sidious and Vader died as the last Sith Lords.

 

Luke and Vader engaged in a lightsaber duel while the Emperor observed from his throne, still encouraging the Jedi apprentice to use the dark side. Luke gave into his anger after Vader learned of his sister's identity and threatened to turn her to the dark side. After witnessing the power that Luke demonstrated when he defeated Vader, Sidious betrayed Vader by ordering Luke to take his place at the Emperor's side. Luke, however, steadfastly refused in turn. Realizing Luke was a true Jedi, and would not be swayed, Sidious attempted to kill him through [torturing](/wiki/Torture "Torture") him with [Force lightning](/wiki/Force_lightning "Force lightning"). However, Vader, torn between his loyalty to his master, his old Jedi connections, and his son, ultimately threw the Emperor down a [reactor](/wiki/Reactor "Reactor") shaft, killing him and returning balance to the Force. With his life-sustaining armor badly damaged from the Emperor's Force lightning, Darth Vader died, but his selfless act allowed him to rejoin the Force as a Force spirit, and be "reborn" as his old self, Anakin Skywalker. Thus, the Sith Order, along with their tyranny was no more,[[43]](#cite_note-Episode_VI-43) as foretold by the ancient prophecy that predicted their downfall.[[139]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-139)

### Interregnum[]

#### Acolytes and new traditions[]

:   "*Through the ages, I've seen evil take many forms. The Sith. The Empire. Today, it is the First Order.*"
:   ―Maz Kanata[[140]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-140)

 [![Despite its destruction, the Sith Order was venerated by various Sith cults throughout the galaxy.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e7/AcolytesOfTheBeyond-SecretsOfTheSith.png/revision/latest?cb=20230108122706) [![Despite its destruction, the Sith Order was venerated by various Sith cults throughout the galaxy.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e7/AcolytesOfTheBeyond-SecretsOfTheSith.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20230108122706)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/e7/AcolytesOfTheBeyond-SecretsOfTheSith.png/revision/latest?cb=20230108122706) 

Despite its destruction, the Sith Order was venerated by various Sith cults throughout the galaxy.

 

While the Sith Order was defeated at the Battle of Endor, it was merely one of many denominations of Force-worshiping religions that existed throughout galactic history. The Sith's ancient legacy as enemies of the Jedi and, at times, rulers of the galaxy, would continue to be felt in the decades that followed its extinction. The downfall of the Sith at Endor left behind a vacuum that others sought to fill, such as the [Knights of Ren](/wiki/Knights_of_Ren "Knights of Ren").[[69]](#cite_note-TFA_VD-69) Thus, while the ancient prophecy that foretold the destruction of the Sith came to pass, it did not foretell the destruction of the darkness, for as long as there existed light, there would always be shadow.[[139]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-139)

Immediately following the deaths of Darth Sidious and Darth Vader, many individuals and groups still adhered to their philosophy. [Yupe Tashu](/wiki/Yupe_Tashu "Yupe Tashu"), an [advisor](/wiki/Emperor%27s_adviser "Emperor's adviser") to the late Sidious, was an admirer of the Sith interrogation methods, as well as their teachings and cunning. He believed that the remaining [Imperial Military](/wiki/Imperial_Military "Imperial Military") had to retreat "beyond the veil of stars," to the Unknown Regions, to search for the source of the dark side that Sidious had come to feel reaching out to him.[[141]](#cite_note-Aftermath-141)[[8]](#cite_note-EE-8) The [Acolytes of the Beyond](/wiki/Acolytes_of_the_Beyond "Acolytes of the Beyond"), who worshiped the Sith, collected [Sith artifacts](/wiki/Sith_artifact "Sith artifact"), such as what they believed to be [Darth Vader's lightsaber](/wiki/Darth_Vader%27s_lightsaber "Darth Vader's lightsaber"), to destroy them, believing this returned the relics to their deceased owners.[[141]](#cite_note-Aftermath-141) The Acolytes eventually collapsed, but one of their members, [Kiza](/wiki/Kiza "Kiza"), was corrupted by the mask of Viceroy Exim Panshard and the promises the dead Sith gave her if she could bring him to Exegol.[[26]](#cite_note-Shadow_of_the_Sith-26)

#### Rieve's charade[]

 [![Rieve adopted a Sith-inspired persona during her time with the Hunters of the Outer Rim.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/37/Rieve-SWHunters.png/revision/latest?cb=20210914232449) [![Rieve adopted a Sith-inspired persona during her time with the Hunters of the Outer Rim.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/37/Rieve-SWHunters.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20210914232449)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/37/Rieve-SWHunters.png/revision/latest?cb=20210914232449) 

Rieve adopted a Sith-inspired persona during her time with the Hunters of the Outer Rim.

 

In [9 ABY](/wiki/9_ABY "9 ABY"),[[142]](#cite_note-9_ABY_Date-142) a Force-sensitive human named [Rieve](/wiki/Rieve "Rieve") joined the competitive sporting show [Hunters of the Outer Rim](/wiki/Hunters_of_the_Outer_Rim "Hunters of the Outer Rim"), where she would adopt the onstage persona of a Sith Lord. In that act,[[143]](#cite_note-BftA-143) she wielded a red lightsaber and owned a suit of [Sith armor](/wiki/Sith_armor "Sith armor") modified to her liking.[[144]](#cite_note-Hunters-144) While in private the two would grow close,[[143]](#cite_note-BftA-143) on stage she had a great rivalry with [J-3DI](/wiki/J-3DI "J-3DI"),[[145]](#cite_note-First_Edition-145) a droid programmed to believe he was a Jedi.[[144]](#cite_note-Hunters-144)

Their rivalry was even made the subject of the first edition of [Arena News](/wiki/Arena_News "Arena News"), where the Arena refreshed fans on the concept of the Sith.[[145]](#cite_note-First_Edition-145) After challenging J-3DI to a battle on one occasion and quickly walking out of interview with Arena announcer [Boz Vega](/wiki/Boz_Vega "Boz Vega"), who claimed to fans Rieve was a Sith Master,[[146]](#cite_note-Rieve's_Wrath-146) Rieve won the "epic battle" against J-3DI, which Arena News claimed brought glory to the Sith. Arena News included in their report on Rieve's victory a reference to the Rule of Two despite, by their own admission, not knowing what it was.[[147]](#cite_note-Powers_of_Dark-147) Rieve made an effort to learn more about the Sith, but she admitted there was not much about the order in the records she reviewed. She did, however, know of Maul and uncovered a reference to his brother Savage Oppress in Sith-related records.[[144]](#cite_note-Hunters-144)

### Rebirth of Darth Sidious[]

#### A sinister plot[]

:   "*At last the work of generations is complete. The great error is corrected. The day of victory is at hand. The day of revenge. The day of the Sith.*"
:   ―Darth Sidious — ![20?cb=20250116042720](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/e/ee/Quote-audio.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20250116042720) [Link](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/12/PalpatinesBroadcast.flac/revision/latest?cb=20250308181525)▶️ ([file info](/wiki/File:PalpatinesBroadcast.flac "File:PalpatinesBroadcast.flac"))[[148]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-148)

 [![Darth Sidious was resurrected when his essence transferred to an imperfect clone of his original body.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/12/SidiousReturns-TROS.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200825054321) [![Darth Sidious was resurrected when his essence transferred to an imperfect clone of his original body.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/12/SidiousReturns-TROS.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200825054321)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/1/12/SidiousReturns-TROS.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200825054321) 

Darth Sidious was resurrected when his essence transferred to an imperfect clone of his original body.

 

Although Darth Sidious perished at Endor, the Sith Lord was able to cheat death, using the dark side of the Force to escape from his falling original body into a cloned body far away from Endor,[[148]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-148) and returned. Sidious settled on the hidden world of the Sith in the [Unknown Regions](/wiki/Unknown_Regions "Unknown Regions"), [Exegol](/wiki/Exegol "Exegol"), along with a cult of followers, the Sith Eternal.[[4]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-4) However, the cloned body was unable to withstand Sidious's power and, as a result, it physically decayed, requiring it to remain connected to cybernetic components, such as an [Ommin harness](/wiki/Ommin_harness "Ommin harness"),[[148]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-148) in order to be sustained and move. On Exegol, the Sith Eternal oversaw the building of the largest [fleet](/wiki/Fleet "Fleet") ever known to the galaxy, the [Final Order](/wiki/Final_Order "Final Order"),[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-15) to establish a resurrected Sith Empire.[[149]](#cite_note-Luke_Gallery-149) Meanwhile, owing to a secret [Contingency](/wiki/Contingency "Contingency") plan designed by Sidious, former [Imperial officers](/wiki/Imperial_officer "Imperial officer"), [nobles](/wiki/Noble "Noble"), and technologists were able to flee into the Unknown Regions, where they established the [First Order](/wiki/First_Order "First Order").[[8]](#cite_note-EE-8)[[150]](#cite_note-Expanded_Edition-150)

 [![Snoke was a strandcast that Darth Sidious created and used as a proxy to rule the First Order.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/30/Snoke_chillin_like_a_villain.png/revision/latest?cb=20180711225254) [![Snoke was a strandcast that Darth Sidious created and used as a proxy to rule the First Order.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/30/Snoke_chillin_like_a_villain.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180711225254)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/30/Snoke_chillin_like_a_villain.png/revision/latest?cb=20180711225254) 

Snoke was a strandcast that Darth Sidious created and used as a proxy to rule the First Order.

 

The Sith Eternal created artificial clone [humanoid](/wiki/Humanoid "Humanoid") [aliens](/wiki/Alien "Alien"), Strand-Casts, and bioengineered abominations[[28]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Sith-28) one of which, [Snoke](/wiki/Snoke "Snoke"),[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-15) came to be [Supreme Leader](/wiki/Supreme_Leader "Supreme Leader") of the First Order,[[140]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-140) though the First Order was unaware of Snoke's true origins nor of the existence of the Sith Eternal[[4]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-4) and the fact that their former Emperor was apparently alive in some form.[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-15) Snoke held a strong connection the dark side of the Force and became a master of its ways,[[150]](#cite_note-Expanded_Edition-150) but was not a Sith himself.[[139]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-139) Such a thing gave him the ability to be a useful pawn for Sidious to use as a way to influence galactic events from the shadows of Exegol, and build [the armies](/wiki/First_Order_military "First Order military") of the First Order,[[28]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Sith-28) with Snoke's knowledge saving the faction from ultimate destruction.[[150]](#cite_note-Expanded_Edition-150)

In [21 ABY](/wiki/21_ABY "21 ABY"),[[151]](#cite_note-21_ABY_Date-151) Skywalker sensed a growing darkness in the Force[[26]](#cite_note-Shadow_of_the_Sith-26) and launched a [quest for Exegol](/wiki/Quest_for_Exegol "Quest for Exegol")[[140]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-140) upon learning from the ghost of his father it was the planet at the center of his visions. At the same time, Kiza and the spirit of Panshard carried on in their own search for Exegol, while the Sith assassin [Ochi](/wiki/Ochi "Ochi") sought out Rey on the orders of the Sith Eternal and Sidious. After [Kiza's death](/wiki/Duel_on_Kiza%27s_world "Duel on Kiza's world") and the [destruction of Panshard's mask](/wiki/Skirmish_on_Taw_Provode "Skirmish on Taw Provode"), which destroyed the Sith viceroy for good, Skywalker believed the disturbance was at an end, but his friend [Landonis Balthazar Calrissian](/wiki/Landonis_Balthazar_Calrissian "Landonis Balthazar Calrissian") elected to stay on the planet [Pasaana](/wiki/Pasaana "Pasaana") for any signs of Ochi, who truly had died in the [Forbidden Valley](/wiki/Forbidden_Valley "Forbidden Valley"), any signs of his daughter [Kadara Calrissian](/wiki/Kadara_Calrissian "Kadara Calrissian"),[[26]](#cite_note-Shadow_of_the_Sith-26) who had been kidnapped by the First Order,[[4]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-4) and any signs of Rey. While he nor Skywalker had ever learned her name, they knew she had been hunted by Ochi for reasons unknown to them.[[26]](#cite_note-Shadow_of_the_Sith-26)

#### The rise of Kylo Ren[]

##### An heir to the Sith[]

:   "*Once reborn as Kylo Ren, he was mine to control. From the shadows, I shaped him into a worthy apprentice—not a true Sith but equally as powerful in the dark side.*"
:   ―Darth Sidious[[28]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Sith-28)

 [![Darth Sidious' machinations brought about the rise of Kylo Ren, whom Snoke trained in the ways of the dark side.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/99/Episode_VIII_Snoke_and_Kylo_Ren.png/revision/latest?cb=20180727071207) [![Darth Sidious' machinations brought about the rise of Kylo Ren, whom Snoke trained in the ways of the dark side.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/99/Episode_VIII_Snoke_and_Kylo_Ren.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20180727071207)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/99/Episode_VIII_Snoke_and_Kylo_Ren.png/revision/latest?cb=20180727071207) 

Darth Sidious' machinations brought about the rise of Kylo Ren, whom Snoke trained in the ways of the dark side.

 

The birth of [Ben Solo](/wiki/Ben_Solo "Ben Solo") presented Darth Sidious with another opportunity to convert a member of the [Skywalker family](/wiki/Skywalker_family "Skywalker family") to the dark side of the Force. As the grandson of Darth Vader, Solo was born with raw and powerful connection to the Force. As such, Sidious planned to turn Solo to the dark side through Snoke, whom he used as a proxy for Solo.[[28]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Sith-28) In time, Snoke turned Solo to the dark side.[[152]](#cite_note-Everything-152) Solo's fall to the dark side occurred after several events, including when he thought his uncle Luke Skywalker tried to kill him,[[153]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-153) a mysterious storm that he summoned and [destroyed](/wiki/Destruction_of_the_Jedi_Temple "Destruction of the Jedi Temple") the [Jedi training temple](/wiki/Jedi_Temple_of_Luke_Skywalker "Jedi Temple of Luke Skywalker"),[[154]](#cite_note-Kylo_Ren_1-154) and when "[Ren](/wiki/Ren_(human) "Ren (human)")" killed his friend [Tai](/wiki/Tai "Tai"). Solo succumbed to darkness, killing Ren, changing his name to Kylo Ren, and becoming the new [master](/wiki/Ren "Ren") of the Knights of Ren, an enclave of dark side users.[[155]](#cite_note-Kylo_Ren_4-155)[[152]](#cite_note-Everything-152) Although Snoke was not a Sith,[[156]](#cite_note-Empire_Interview-156) he was strong with the Force. Snoke took Ren as his apprentice and trained him in the ways of the dark side, but Sidious considered himself to be the true master of Ren.[[28]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Sith-28) Elsewhere, Skywalker went into a self-imposed exile, his location unknown to the galaxy.[[140]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-140)

 [![Kylo Ren's path to power through the dark side was inspired by the legacy of Darth Vader, his grandfather.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/79/Kylo_Ren_Vader_Helmet_Chamber.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160420020932) [![Kylo Ren's path to power through the dark side was inspired by the legacy of Darth Vader, his grandfather.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/79/Kylo_Ren_Vader_Helmet_Chamber.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20160420020932)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/7/79/Kylo_Ren_Vader_Helmet_Chamber.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20160420020932) 

Kylo Ren's path to power through the dark side was inspired by the legacy of Darth Vader, his grandfather.

 

Kylo Ren pledged to finish what his grandfather Darth Vader had begun, although Supreme Leader Snoke scorned the sentimentality of Vader, which he believed had led to the Empire's downfall. Ultimately, Ren hoped to build an immunity to the light, and succeed where Vader failed.[[157]](#cite_note-TFA_N-157) Luke Skywalker, Ren's former master and the last Jedi, once blamed the Jedi Order for Darth Sidious' rise to power.[[153]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-153) Unbeknownst to Ren, his training in the dark side was monitored by Sidious. The Dark Lord regarded Ren as a worthy apprentice and the heir to Vader. Although he did not view Ren as a true Sith, Sidious confirmed that Ren was powerful with the dark side nonetheless.[[28]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Sith-28) Ren was a [warlord](/wiki/Warlord "Warlord") and champion of the First Order[[158]](#cite_note-Kylo_Ren_DB-158) by the time of the [First Order-Resistance War](/wiki/First_Order-Resistance_War "First Order-Resistance War"), a galactic conflict that ensued between the First Order and the [Resistance](/wiki/Resistance "Resistance") in the aftermath of the [New Republic](/wiki/New_Republic "New Republic")'s [destruction](/wiki/Hosnian_Cataclysm "Hosnian Cataclysm")[[140]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-140) in [34 ABY](/wiki/34_ABY "34 ABY").[[42]](#cite_note-GA-42) During the First Order's initial invasion of the known galaxy from the Unknown Regions,[[139]](#cite_note-TLJ_VD-139) Ren discovered that he shared a powerful [Force-bond](/wiki/Force-bond "Force-bond") with [Rey](/wiki/Rey_Skywalker "Rey Skywalker"), a Force-sensitive [scavenger](/wiki/Scavenger "Scavenger") from [Jakku](/wiki/Jakku "Jakku"), whom Luke Skywalker instructed in the ways of the Jedi.[[153]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-153)

Their connection led Rey to believe that Ben Solo could be redeemed from the dark side; although they succeeded in destroying Snoke and his [Praetorian Guards](/wiki/Praetorian_Guard "Praetorian Guard") during the [Battle of Oetchi](/wiki/Battle_of_Oetchi "Battle of Oetchi"), Kylo Ren not only remained committed to the dark side, he usurped his master's title as Supreme Leader of the First Order. Ren denounced the legacies of both Jedi and Sith. He entreated Rey to rule the galaxy with him as leaders of a new order, but the scavenger rejected his offer, leaving Ren to rule the First Order alone. Ren attempted to annihilate his enemies during the [Battle of Crait](/wiki/Battle_of_Crait "Battle of Crait"), having vowed to destroy the past and all elements of defiance to his rule, but through the [sacrifice](/wiki/Force_projection "Force projection") of Luke Skywalker, Rey and the Resistance escaped from Ren's forces.[[153]](#cite_note-Episode_VIII-153)

##### The legacy of Darth Vader[]

:   "*Darth Vader never allowed himself to forget his past, filled with horrors though it was. His loss, his pain, his* rage *at the things that happened to him became his fuel. He never looked back, but he never let go either. This is why the dark side ran so strongly through him. I can tell you how he did it. I can tell you how he turned his past…into his* power*. You* need *this, boy. You wouldn't have come here if you didn't. You're* lost*.*"
:   ―Vaneé, to Kylo Ren[[159]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vader_1-159)

 [![Kylo Ren would undertake a journey to discover the history of his grandfather, hoping to learn how Darth Vader converted his pain into a source of dark power.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/92/Legacy-of-Vader-1-Textless-Cover.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20250117173017) [![Kylo Ren would undertake a journey to discover the history of his grandfather, hoping to learn how Darth Vader converted his pain into a source of dark power.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/92/Legacy-of-Vader-1-Textless-Cover.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20250117173017)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/9/92/Legacy-of-Vader-1-Textless-Cover.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20250117173017) 

Kylo Ren would undertake a journey to discover the history of his grandfather, hoping to learn how Darth Vader converted his pain into a source of dark power.

 

Kylo Ren was not a Sith,[[28]](#cite_note-Secrets_of_the_Sith-28) yet his training in the dark side was based on Sith teachings and practices, such as the Sith trial of ascendancy which Ren completed by killing his father, [Han Solo](/wiki/Han_Solo "Han Solo"), in an act of patricide.[[4]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-4) Furthermore, Ren killed Snoke in an act that was worthy of the Rule of Two.[[160]](#cite_note-The_Dark_Side-160) However, not even Snoke's death succeeded in ending the conflict within Ren, who was a product of both Jedi and Sith teachings.[[158]](#cite_note-Kylo_Ren_DB-158) In spite of his efforts, he struggled to resist the pull to light that prevented him from fully surrendering to the dark side. Ren looked to the memory of his grandfather, Darth Vader, as a source of inspiration for his own journey to the dark side, yet he remained fearful of never growing as strong as Vader.[[140]](#cite_note-Episode_VII-140) However, by the time of his accession as Supreme Leader, Ren was no longer certain that he wanted to follow in Vader's path.[[159]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vader_1-159) In turning to the dark side, Ren had forsaken all that he once cherished in exchange for an isolated existence—devoid of love and friendship—that he spent with a master whom he hated and followers that he did not trust.[[4]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-4)

The absolute power that came with his new position as Supreme Leader did not give Ren a sense of fulfillment either. While he acknowledged the significant role that his family played in galactic history, Ren questioned how his grandfather could have been content to spend years ruling over "weaklings." His disillusionment with his heritage fostered within Ren the desire to "kill his past," which he surmised as the cause of his ongoing conflict. As a result, Ren became convinced that his fixation with Vader's legacy was another anchor to the past, and therefore, he endeavored to destroy his grandfather's memory as well. But upon meeting [Vaneé](/wiki/Vane%C3%A9 "Vaneé") in Fortress Vader on Mustafar, Ren became tempted by the prospect of learning how his grandfather channeled the pain of his past into power with the dark side. Vaneé mocked Ren's rejection of his legacy, but having spent a lifetime in service to the Dark Lord of the Sith, he offered to serve the grandson and heir of his late master.[[159]](#cite_note-Legacy_of_Vader_1-159)

#### The final downfall[]

:   "*You are nothing! A scavenger girl is no match for the power in me. I am* all *the Sith!*""*And I… I'm all the Jedi.*"
:   ―Darth Sidious and Rey[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-15)

 [![The Final Order was discovered by Ren when he confronted the Emperor in his citadel on Exegol.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d5/GraphicNovel-Sith-Statues.png/revision/latest?cb=20211008131439) [![The Final Order was discovered by Ren when he confronted the Emperor in his citadel on Exegol.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d5/GraphicNovel-Sith-Statues.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20211008131439)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/d/d5/GraphicNovel-Sith-Statues.png/revision/latest?cb=20211008131439) 

The Final Order was discovered by Ren when he confronted the Emperor in his citadel on Exegol.

 

In the [year](/wiki/35_ABY "35 ABY") that followed,[[4]](#cite_note-TROS_VD-4) Supreme Leader Kylo Ren found Exegol, where he discovered Sidious, the Sith Eternal and its fleet, the Final Order, which he planned to unleash on the galaxy in order to establish a new Sith Empire. He further revealed to Ren that Rey was his granddaughter as the daughter of his [son](/wiki/Dathan "Dathan") and his son's [wife](/wiki/Miramir "Miramir"), both of whom Sidious had killed. Sidious offered Ren the Sith fleet and a new Sith Empire if he killed Rey. Ren later informed the [First Order Supreme Council](/wiki/First_Order_Supreme_Council "First Order Supreme Council") of the existence of the Sith fleet. [Allegiant General](/wiki/Allegiant_General "Allegiant General") [Enric Pryde](/wiki/Enric_Pryde "Enric Pryde") believed it could be used to increase their forces tenfold for their ultimate push towards galactic conquest. After Ren abandoned the First Order, General Pryde, a veteran of the Old Empire, was given command of the Sith fleet for swearing fealty to Sidious.[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-15)

Rey arrived on Exegol to confront her grandfather in his throne room before an amphitheater of his followers, who chanted as Sidious spoke. Sidious told Rey he never planned to kill her, having manipulated Ren, but instead wanted her to take his place on the Sith throne. Sidious pressured her to sacrifice him, planning to use an esoteric power to transfer his spirit into her body.[[148]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-148) During his temptation, Sidious showed Rey the unveiling [Battle of Exegol](/wiki/Battle_of_Exegol "Battle of Exegol"), which erupted as a result of Rey sending the coordinates to Exegol to her friends in the Resistance. Although the Resistance was initially outnumbered by the Sith Eternal forces, they were reinforced by a [Citizens' Fleet](/wiki/Citizens%27_Fleet "Citizens' Fleet").[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-15)

 [![With his strength restored, the Emperor assured his followers that the return of the Sith was inevitable.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/07/Sidious_triumphant.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20250205185007) [![With his strength restored, the Emperor assured his followers that the return of the Sith was inevitable.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/07/Sidious_triumphant.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20250205185007)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/0/07/Sidious_triumphant.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20250205185007) 

With his strength restored, the Emperor assured his followers that the return of the Sith was inevitable.

 

A returned Ben Solo arrived on Exegol, who went on to defeat the Knights of Ren and accompany Rey, standing side-by-side against the Dark Lord of the Sith. Sidious angrily grabbed the two using the Force and inadvertently drew some of their life force, which caused his body to begin healing; realizing that their connection was a dyad in the Force, Sidious [siphoned](/wiki/Force_drain "Force drain") the life force of their bond to rejuvenate his body. Out of pure spite for the Skywalker bloodline, Sidious disposed of Solo into a nearby abyss. Sidious ascended the throne of the Sith, and used Force lightning to attack the Resistance and citizens' fleet.[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-15)

 [![The Sith tradition perished with the destruction of Darth Sidious and his followers during the Battle of Exegol.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a9/The_death_of_Sidious.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200401233403) [![The Sith tradition perished with the destruction of Darth Sidious and his followers during the Battle of Exegol.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a9/The_death_of_Sidious.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20200401233403)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/a/a9/The_death_of_Sidious.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20200401233403) 

The Sith tradition perished with the destruction of Darth Sidious and his followers during the Battle of Exegol.

 

Rey, strengthened by the spirits of the past Jedi, arose. Sidious proceeded to direct his lightning towards her, intent on killing her, but Rey defended herself with Anakin and Leia's lightsabers, deflecting the lightning back at Sidious, who disintegrated, destroying the Sith and unleashing an explosion that caused the entire amphitheater to crumble. Rey died, but Solo survived and climbed out of the pit, where he found Rey lifeless on the ground. Crawling to her, Solo gave his life force to resurrect her, and died shortly thereafter. Rey ultimately rejected her [dark ancestry](/wiki/Palpatine_family "Palpatine family"); she took the Skywalker surname to honor the extinct [Skywalker family](/wiki/Skywalker_family "Skywalker family") and remained a Jedi, permanently preventing the return of the Sith.[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-15)

Without the Sith, the First Order faced a series of attacks as people [rose up](/wiki/Uprising_against_the_First_Order "Uprising against the First Order") across the galaxy, inspired by the victory of the Resistance and the citizens' fleet at Exegol.[[15]](#cite_note-Episode_IX-15)[[161]](#cite_note-Leia_Gallery-161)

## Behind the scenes[]

:   "*The Sith are people who are very self-centered and selfish. There used to be many Sith, but because they were corrupted by power and ambition, they killed each other off, so now there are only two - a master and an apprentice. Sith rely on their passion to get things done. They use their raw emotion, their hatred, their anger, their bitterness - which is the dark side of the Force. The Force is what binds the galaxy together, and it has a good side and a bad side. The Sith learned how to manipulate both sides of the Force, and then they fell into the trap of being corrupted by the dark side. The Jedi Knights are like marshals in the Wild West. It's their job to make sure everyone is protected, to bring peace. They are the enemy of the Sith, because the Sith want to dominate the galaxy, to control everything, and for a thousand years they have had a plot against the Jedi. So, in this movie, it is time for them to seek revenge against the Jedi for perceived injustices and to carry out that plot.*"
:   ―George Lucas on the Sith in [*Star Wars*: Episode III *Revenge of the Sith*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_III_Revenge_of_the_Sith "Star Wars: Episode III Revenge of the Sith")[[162]](#cite_note-162)

 [![Sith was first mentioned in the 1976 novelization of Star Wars.](data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3a/FromtheAdventuresofLukeSkywalker.png/revision/latest?cb=20190926173352) [![Sith was first mentioned in the 1976 novelization of Star Wars.](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3a/FromtheAdventuresofLukeSkywalker.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/200?cb=20190926173352)](https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/starwars/images/3/3a/FromtheAdventuresofLukeSkywalker.png/revision/latest?cb=20190926173352) 

Sith was first mentioned in the 1976 novelization of *Star Wars*.

 

The Sith first appeared as the primary antagonists of [George Lucas](/wiki/George_Lucas "George Lucas")' [Original trilogy](/wiki/Original_trilogy "Original trilogy") and the [Prequel trilogy](/wiki/Prequel_trilogy "Prequel trilogy"). In the [1975](/wiki/1975 "1975") [second draft](/wiki/Adventures_of_the_Starkiller,_Episode_I:_The_Star_Wars "Adventures of the Starkiller, Episode I: The Star Wars") for *[A New Hope](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_IV_A_New_Hope "Star Wars: Episode IV A New Hope")*, the Sith are introduced as the "Black Knights of the Sith", a sect of mercenary warriors who used the "Bogan", the evil, dark side of the "Force of Others". According to the story, the Sith once were pirates, taught to the way of the evil side by a fallen "Padawan-Jedi" called Darklighter.[[163]](#cite_note-The_Making_of_Star_Wars:_The_Definitive_Story_Behind_the_Original_Film-163) "Sith" is used in the [1976 novelization of *Star Wars*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_A_New_Hope_(novelization) "Star Wars: A New Hope (novelization)") as part of a title for the key villain [Darth Vader](/wiki/Anakin_Skywalker "Anakin Skywalker"), the "Dark Lord of the Sith," a term cut from the original film. [*The Phantom Menace*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_I_The_Phantom_Menace "Star Wars: Episode I The Phantom Menace"), which premiered in [1999](/wiki/1999 "1999"), was the first film to use the word proper, and established key concepts including the Rule of Two. In addition, the origins and history of the Sith was explored by several non-[canon](/wiki/Canon "Canon") [Star Wars Legends](/wiki/Star_Wars_Legends "Star Wars Legends") works including the [1993](/wiki/1993 "1993")-[1998](/wiki/1998 "1998") [Dark Horse Comics](/wiki/Dark_Horse_Comics "Dark Horse Comics") [*Star Wars: Tales of the Jedi*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Tales_of_the_Jedi_(comic_series) "Star Wars: Tales of the Jedi (comic series)") comics, the [2003](/wiki/2003 "2003") [BioWare](/wiki/BioWare "BioWare") game *[Star Wars: Knights of the Old Republic](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Knights_of_the_Old_Republic "Star Wars: Knights of the Old Republic")* and [its](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Knights_of_the_Old_Republic_II:_The_Sith_Lords "Star Wars: Knights of the Old Republic II: The Sith Lords") [sequels](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Old_Republic "Star Wars: The Old Republic"), [Drew Karpyshyn](/wiki/Drew_Karpyshyn "Drew Karpyshyn")'s [*Darth Bane Trilogy*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Darth_Bane_Trilogy "Star Wars: Darth Bane Trilogy"), the *[Star Wars: Legacy](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Legacy "Star Wars: Legacy")* comic series, and [John Jackson Miller](/wiki/John_Jackson_Miller "John Jackson Miller")'s [*Lost Tribe of the Sith*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Lost_Tribe_of_the_Sith "Star Wars: Lost Tribe of the Sith") novellas. More recently, the canon television series *[Star Wars: The Clone Wars](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Clone_Wars "Star Wars: The Clone Wars")* and *[Star Wars Rebels](/wiki/Star_Wars_Rebels "Star Wars Rebels")* have touched upon the origins and history of the Sith.

[Sam Witwer](/wiki/Sam_Witwer "Sam Witwer"), who has voiced Maul and Sidious in animation, opined the Sith do not believe in life after death. That is why they go to such extreme lengths to survive. However, the Jedi will sacrifice themselves as they believe their deaths can inspire others. "You have Darth Vader, who lives a terrible life, he lives a pathetic, tortured existence but it's still preferable to having nothing, which is how he views death. The same thing with Darth Sidious, you look at him in *Return of the Jedi*. He's over 100 years old and is a bent, old man. But that's better than the alternative, which is nothing."[[164]](#cite_note-164) An appearance from the Force spirits of Darth Bane and [Revan](/wiki/Revan/Legends "Revan/Legends") in "[Ghosts of Mortis](/wiki/Ghosts_of_Mortis "Ghosts of Mortis")" was removed at the last minute by George Lucas since the Sith returning after death conflicted with his views on the Force.[[165]](#cite_note-SW-Ghosts_of_Mortis_Episode_Featurette-165) As it shown in later episodes, transcending death as a Force spirit could only be achieved via the light side.[[166]](#cite_note-Voices-166)[[167]](#cite_note-Destiny_(The_Clone_Wars)-167)[[17]](#cite_note-Sacrifice-17) Nonetheless, members of the Sith sought to escape death through other means,[[14]](#cite_note-Dark_Lord_of_the_Sith_22-14) including Darth Sidious himself in both canon[[148]](#cite_note-TROS_EE-148) and in the Expanded Universe.[[168]](#cite_note-Dark_Empire_2-168)

According to *[Shadow of the Sith](/wiki/Shadow_of_the_Sith "Shadow of the Sith")* author [Adam Christopher](/wiki/Adam_Christopher "Adam Christopher"), the Sith were not always an organized faction; at such a time, the title "Darth" did not exist. Christopher believes the Sith Lord Exim Panshard came from this era.[[169]](#cite_note-Predate_Organized-169) In the non-Canon animated television series *[LEGO Star Wars: The Freemaker Adventures](/wiki/LEGO_Star_Wars:_The_Freemaker_Adventures "LEGO Star Wars: The Freemaker Adventures")*, the primary antagonist [Naare](/wiki/Naare "Naare") is identified as a Sith agent of Darth Sidious and Darth Vader.[[170]](#cite_note-A_Hero_Discovered-170) The non-canon comic [*Visions – Peach Momoko* 1](/wiki/Visions_%E2%80%93_Peach_Momoko_1 "Visions – Peach Momoko 1") features the [Ankok](/wiki/Ankok "Ankok"), a cult dedicated to a deceased Sith Lord.[[171]](#cite_note-Peach_Momoko_1-171)

[↑](#cite_ref-TROS_Date_44-0) *[Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker: The Visual Dictionary](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Rise_of_Skywalker:_The_Visual_Dictionary "Star Wars: The Rise of Skywalker: The Visual Dictionary")* dates the events of *Star Wars*: Episode IX *The Rise of Skywalker* as taking place one [year](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") after the [Starkiller Incident](/wiki/Hosnian_Cataclysm "Hosnian Cataclysm"), which *[Star Wars: Galactic Atlas](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Galactic_Atlas "Star Wars: Galactic Atlas")* dates to [34 ABY](/wiki/34_ABY "34 ABY"). Therefore, the events of *Star Wars*: Episode IX *The Rise of Skywalker* must take place in [35 ABY](/wiki/35_ABY "35 ABY"). 45. [↑](#cite_ref-Destiny_Acolyte_99-0) [The Acolyte logo Celebration](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Acolyte "Star Wars: The Acolyte") *[Star Wars: The Acolyte](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Acolyte "Star Wars: The Acolyte")* — "[Destiny](/wiki/Destiny_(The_Acolyte) "Destiny (The Acolyte)")" 100. ↑ [100.0](#cite_ref-148_Date_100-0) [100.1](#cite_ref-148_Date_100-1) [StarWars.com](/wiki/StarWars.com "StarWars.com") ["Lost/Found" Episode Guide | The Acolyte](https://www.starwars.com/series/the-acolyte/lost-found-episode-guide) on [StarWars.com](/wiki/StarWars.com "StarWars.com") ([backup link](https://web.archive.org/web/20240613105150/https://www.starwars.com/series/the-acolyte/lost-found-episode-guide)) states that the events of *[Star Wars: The Acolyte](/wiki/Star_Wars:_The_Acolyte "Star Wars: The Acolyte")* take place 100 [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") before the events of [*Star Wars*: Episode I *The Phantom Menace*](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Episode_I_The_Phantom_Menace "Star Wars: Episode I The Phantom Menace"), which *[Star Wars: Timelines](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Timelines "Star Wars: Timelines")* dates to [32 BBY](/wiki/32_BBY "32 BBY"). Therefore, *The Acolyte* takes place in [132 BBY](/wiki/132_BBY "132 BBY").      "[Destiny](/wiki/Destiny_(The_Acolyte) "Destiny (The Acolyte)")" dates itself to sixteen [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") before the series' main events, equating to [148 BBY](/wiki/148_BBY "148 BBY"). 101. [↑](#cite_ref-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost_Date_104-0) *[Star Wars: Absolutely Everything You Need to Know](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Absolutely_Everything_You_Need_to_Know "Star Wars: Absolutely Everything You Need to Know")* gives the age of [Dooku](/wiki/Dooku "Dooku") at the [time](/wiki/Time "Time") of the [First Battle of Geonosis](/wiki/First_Battle_of_Geonosis "First Battle of Geonosis") as eighty [years](/wiki/Standard_year "Standard year") old. *[Star Wars: Galactic Atlas](/wiki/Star_Wars:_Galactic_Atlas "Star Wars: Galactic Atlas")* dates the Battle of [Geonosis](/wiki/Geonosis "Geonosis") to [22 BBY](/wiki/22_BBY "22 BBY"), placing Dooku's [birth](/wiki/Reproduction "Reproduction") year in [102 BBY](/wiki/102_BBY "102 BBY"). The [script](/wiki/Dooku:_Jedi_Lost_(script) "Dooku: Jedi Lost (script)") of *[Dooku: Jedi Lost](/wiki/Dooku:_Jedi_Lost "Dooku: Jedi Lost")* states that Dooku is twenty years old during the [mission](/wiki/Mission_to_Asusto "Mission to Asusto") to [Asusto](/wiki/Asusto "Asusto"), meaning that the mission must have occurred in [82 BBY](/wiki/82_BBY "82 BBY"). 105. ↑ [105.0](#cite_ref-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost_script_105-0) [105.1](#cite_ref-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost_script_105-1) [105.2](#cite_ref-Dooku:_Jedi_Lost_script_105-2) [*Dooku: Jedi Lost* script](/wiki/Dooku:_Jedi_Lost_(script) "Dooku: Jedi Lost (script)") 106.
